chung la btang ba/ p. 9916 bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i mkhyen pa mnga' yang tha mal pa ltar mdzad pa/ p. 10017 gdul rgyud dam pa'i chos ci 'byor du sbyor ba/ p. 10118 mi mthun

pa/ p. 16926 ma 'ongs pa'i dus kyang rnam par thar pa rgyun mi 'chad pa/ p. 173

/ / dpal ldan bla ma dam pa mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa don gyi slad du mtshan nas smos te gzhon nu dpal gyi rnam par thar pa yon tan rin po che mchog tu rgyas pa'i ljon
pa zhes bya ba bzhugs so/ /

1 mchod par brjod pa dang mtshams sbyor ba/thugs rje mtshungs pa med pa'i bla ma dang sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la gus pa chen pos phyag 'tshal lo/ sngon
gyi bskal pa mang por rlabs chen tshogs gnyis spyod pa du ma spyad pa las/ sku tshe 'dir yang gzhon nu nyid nas byang chub sems dpa'i rigs kyi rtags rnams dang / skye
bas thob pa'i mkhyen rab phul byung ldog pa med pa'i brtson 'grus phun tshogs pas/ snyigs ma'i dus su thub dbang bstan pa yongs su rdzogs pa'i dpal mnga' la phyag 'tshal/
gang gi mkhyen pas gsung rab dgongs 'grel dang bcas phyogs 'dir bzhugs rnams kun mkhyen nas/ gzhan la brtse bas legs bshad mtha' dag dpe 'khyud med par brtse ba'i dgongs
pas rjes su ston/ rgyal ba'i 'phrin las 'phel ba la dgyes mdo sngags brtsom pa'i 'phrin las rmad du byung / mchog gi bla ma lung rtogs yon tan khur gyis lci bas bla ma'i
bla mar 'dud/ rje btsun rnam thar bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i/ rin chen ljon pa mdor bstan yal ga rnams/ rgyal bshad 'dab ma 'bras bzang du mas mdzes/ dad mos sa chen spo las
mngon par 'khrungs/ de yang bdag cag gis yongs su 'dzin pa chen po de ni/ sku'i skye ba snga ma mang por rlabs che'i spyod pa rab tu spyad pa/ sku'i skye ba 'dir yang
kha na ma tho ba med pa'i rigs su 'khrungs pa/ rgyal ba rnams kyi rjes su zhugs pa yongs su rdzogs pa/ sngon gyi dge ba'i

bag chags bzang pos rigs sad pa'i skyes bu chen po/ mkhas shing grub pa'i skyes bu drug bcu rtsa drug la brten nas thos bsam phyogs med du mdzad pa/ rnam par dag pa'i dam tshig
la nan tan du mdzad pas bla ma rnams kyis byin gyis brlabs pa/ bsams pa las byung ba'i shes rab kyi klong phyogs med du brdol ba/ yon tan thams cad la gong nas gong
du 'gyur legs par thon pa/ mtho dman gyi skye bo thams cad la sngon ji lta ba bzhin du 'grogs pa'i gzhung bzang ba/ mched grogs dang slob ma dang 'khor dang nye phyogs su
bzod pa'i go cha sra ba/ chos zab mo la bzod pa rab tu thob pa/ pha rol tu phyin pa dang gsang sngags kyi phyogs la po ti 'di tsam zhig mkhyen pa yin zer ba'i tshad sus
kyang bzung bar mi nus pa/ spobs pa'i mtha' gang la'ang gtugs pa med pa/ bas mtha'i gnas rnams su bzhugs te zab pa dang rgya che ba'i chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu skor nas gdul
bya yongs su smin par mdzad pa/ 'jig rten gyi gtam sna tshogs la gtso bor ma mdzad par dam pa'i chos kyi 'brel ba'i gtam kho nas dus 'da' bar mdzad pa/ dge ba'i gshes
gnyen su la'ang phrag mi dog par yang dag pa'i bstod pa mdzad pa/ dman pa rnams la 'ang brnyas par mi mdzad pa/ sku'i spyod pa rnams shin du gtsang ba/ mdzad spyod thams
cad mtha' gnyis dang bral bar spyod pa/ 'jig rten gyi rnam g.yeng thams cad je chung je chung la btang nas bya bral gyi brtul zhugs je bzang je bzang du gtong ba/ bsam gyis
mi khyab pa'i mkhyen pa mnga' yang tha mal pa ltar mdzad pa/ gdul bar bya ba ji snyed pa'i rgyud dam pa'i chos dang ci 'byor du sbyor ba/ snyan pa'i grags pas phyogs kun
du khyab pas che dgu thams cad kyis zhabs kyi padmar phyag byas pa/ mi mthun?'thun pa'i phyogs thams cad sgyu ma lta bu dang rjes su 'thun pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyis bzlog
par nus pa/ spyir snyigs ma'i dus 'dir sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la bya ba rgya chen po dang / bye brag tu 'gyur dang yig 'jog mang du gnang bas bstanapa gsal bar mdzad
pa/ zab pa dang rgya che ba'i gsung gi rgyun thams cad skyes bu chen po

rnams kyis rjes su bzlos pa'i phrin las phun sum tshogs pa dang ldan pa/ gsol ba ji ltar btab pa bzhin du yun du bzhugs par bzhed pa'i thugs rje chen po mnga' ba/ mnal lam
gyi 'jug pa yang sgyu ma'i rnam 'phrul ltar spyod par nus pa/ sgrib pa med pa'i chos kyi sgo phul du byung ba mngon du brnyes pa/ slob ma mchog dman bar ma'i skal ba dang
mtshams pa'i chos ston pa la ngal ba mi mnga' ba/ ma 'ongs pa'i dus kyang sems dpa' chen po'i rnam par thar pa rgyun mi 'chad pa zhes bya ba ni/ rags pa'i sde tshan rnam
par dbye ba'i mdor bstan gyi yal gas phyug par gyur pa nyid do/ / da ni de rnams rgyas par bshad pa'i 'dab ma rab tu rgyas shing don bzang po'i 'bras bus mngon par brjid
pa spros te brjod pa la/ 2 sku'i skye ba snga ma mang por rlabs po che'i sbyod pa rab tu spyad pa zhes bya ba ni/grub chen u rgyan pa'i slob ma go lung pa gzhon nu dpal
du gyur to zhes bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi bya ba btang ba'i brtul zhugs la gnas pa sha stag tu 'khrungs pa las 'di ni brgya dang bcu bdun pa yin no/ zhes lhag pa'i lhas
mnal lam du lung bstan pa dang / bsam yas su phyin pa'i tshe/ khyad par du dad pa 'phel zhing dang po sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa 'dzugs pa'i dus su nges par bya ba rnams la
gtogs pa zhig yin bsam pa skye ba zhig yong gi 'dugasu yin ni mi shes bstan pa 'dzugs pa'i dus su nges par bsam yas su skyes pa 'dra gsung zhing / bsam yas bzhengs pa'i
lo rgyus dang / rgyal blon rnams kyi bya ba ji ltar mdzad pa dang / mkhan po bo dhi sa twa dang slob dpon padma phebs nas bstan pa btsugs pa dang / lo tsA ba chen po rnams
kyis chos ji ltar bsgyur ba gsung dus spyan chab mang du 'byin zhing / gus pa'i rnam 'gyur cher mdzad pa dang / snar thang nas jo mo nang mjal du phebs pa'i phyir lam/
brag ram du byon/ de ni se ba mang du 'dug pa la se 'bru rnams mthus/ gtsug lag khang der phebs nas bzhugs pas de'i tho skor gyi skye bo rnams kyi tsam pa dang dar ba la
sogs mang du khyer nas 'bul du byung / der phebs ma thag nas de rnams su shin du bag phebs pa dang yul yin pa snyam byed pa dang / gtsug lag khang de'i nang du phebs pa
tsam gyis sngar 'dris rgyus yod pa snyam byed pa dang / ka gdong 'di rnams su yangachos kyi bshad pa la

sogs pa chos phyogs kyi bya ba mang po zhig bdag gis byas pa yin snyam pa'ang yun ring bar byung / brag ram der yang nges par skyes pa 'dug gsung / 'ji lha khang stengs su
bzhugs pa'i tshe bla ma bkra shis bsod nams pa zhes bya ba'i rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug skyes bu dam pa/ dus kyi 'khor lo la sogs pa'i sku yon tan shin du che ba/ khrid kyis
gdul bya smin par mdzad pa de la sogs pa la chos gsungs tshe khong gi gsung nas drung pa bcom ldan rigs ral yin snyam du yang yang nyams la 'ong ba zhig byung zhus par
'dug cing / bdag gi bla ma mtshungs med nam mkha' blo gros kyi zhal snga nas ni/ kho bo'i bla ma dam pa 'di dpal phag mo grub pa dpon slob kyi skor de na bzhugs pa zhig
cis kyang yin bsam pa yod gsung / chos rje rin po che lo chen gyi zhal nas/ mdo sngags thams cad la mkhyen pa mtha' yas shing / lo tswa byang ba dang de'i rtsom pa rnams
la'ang dgyes par snang bas/ nges par rong zom chos kyi bzang po'i sku skye yin pa 'dra zhes bdag la yang yang gsungango / / mkhyen pa dang mdzad pa'i tshul gang la brtags
kyang sku'i skye ba snga ma ma mang por nges par sbyangs pa chen po mnga' ba zhig ste/ rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po slob dpon rdor bzang pa zhes bya ba'i mi phyed pa'i dad
pa dang ldan pa de la/ zhal snga nas/ slob dpon pa khyed nga'i yon tan rnams la ci sems gsung / sku yon tan ngas dpag par ga la nus/ sku skye 'di kho nar sbyangs pa'i sku
yon yin bsam pa cig ma byung zhus pas/ ha ha de skad byas chog pa lta bur yang 'dug ngas rgyud bla ma 'di dang por blo la bzung ste zin pa dang go ba mnyam du byung nas
slob gnyer gsar du byed ma dgos/ dus phyis su song nas kyang zhib cha kha yar la blo bskyed ni byung / gzhan dang po rang shar ba de bsgyur ma dgos gsung / de 'dra ba'i tshul
gzhan yang mang du yod pa 'dra zhes slopa dpon smon lam grags pas/ rje nyid kyi gsung zin bris su btab pa las byung ngo /3 sku'i skye ba 'dir yang kha na ma tho ba med
pa'i rigs du 'khrungs pa zhes bya ba ni/zhal snga nas nged tsho bod rgyal po'i blon po 'gos rgan gyi rgyud pa yin/ 'gos yul 'bring mtshams nas chad par 'dug gsung ste/
yab mes snga mo'i dus su?du dbus su lhags nas/ rgya sman yang po sar phebs te yang po'i lho'i gad pa

dam pa 'di'i stengs su nged kyi pha mtsher gyi ra ba zhig gtsigs pa yin zer nas bzung pas ngam pa rar grags te de nas mang du mched/ yab mes snga mo'i mi cig 'ju phu'i co btsan
gyi 'khor du skyes nas de mi rnams kyis mthong bar nang du 'ong / de la lto skom ster kho'i lham sdogs kyang 'debs dgos/ res lto za 'phro la chu byang khar co btsan
dpon g.yog byon zer 'gro ba yang yod/ dus phyi zhig na a mi kun rgyal zhes bya ba byung / de la spun zla bsam rdor dang grags bzang bya ba yod de/ grags bzang gi rgyud da
lta'i khyu ma ba 'di rnams yin/ bsam rdor gyi rgyud la bsod rgyal zhes bya ba'i dge bshes blo gsal zhig yod pa la mched zla lta bur dgongs te thugs rjes bzung na'ang gzhon
nu la 'das/ yang a mi sangs rgyas skyabs shes bya ba la bu dpon kun dang slob dpon sang grags pa gnyis/ gzhan ma mi gcig pa cig dang gsum byung ba'i dpon kun gyi rgyud
rnams ra mo che dang chos 'khor gling sogs skyid shod du gzhi 'chas/ slob dpon sang grags pa ni yab la longs spyod med par sgye gcig dang phor ba gcig bsnams nas spyan g.yas
su byon/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan pa'i zhabs la gtugs nas rab tu byung / sgos kyi slob dpon shes rab dpal ba la brten nas spyod 'jug la slob gnyer mdzad pas
legs par mkhyen nas/ phyis 'chad nyan kyang mdzad/ dkar nag gi rtsis dang gshin po rjes su 'dzin pa'i cho ga la sogs pa yon tan du ma dang ldan pa byon te/ drug bcu rtsa
drug pa bya'i lo la gshegs/ kun rgyal la bu 'byung gnas rdo rje zhes bya ba 'jig rten gyi lo rgyus la sogs smrabazang ba zhig byung ste/ ston ming ston pa 'byung gnas
rdo rje zhes kyang bya/ de 'og bsam gtan 'phel te gzhon nu la 'das/ de 'og ston pa tshul khrims bsam grub bo/ 'byung gnas rdo rje dang sri thar skyid gnyis la sras lnga dang
sras mo gsum byung ba'i sras che bas khyim gzung ste ring po ma lon par 'das/ de 'og kyang snga mor 'das/ bzhi pa bla ma nam mkha' bzang ste/ thugs rab che zhing skyes
bu dam pa mang po'i zhabs la gtugs nas bsgom chos mang du zhus/ lnga pa slob dpon mgon rdor ro/ bu mo che

ba rdo rje skyid/ de 'og bu 'dren/ de 'og rin chen skyid rnams so/ chos rje rin po che ni sras gsum pa ste/ rgya sman lha khang gi mda' grong nag mo/ de'i nang nas kyang dbus
khyim zhes bya bar chu pho spre'u'i lo spyi lo 1392la sku bltams pa/ ring po ma lon par yab kyis na bzas btums nas khur te spyan g.yas su byon pa'i lam rtsig kha cig tu
bzhugs su bcug nas yab kyis khams bsang ba thugs kyis dran/ de rjes gzhan ni ma dran par snang yang khams shin tu dwangs pa yod pa'i rtags su 'dug gsung / yab snga mo nas
mi lag tu song bas yum gyis legs par bskyangs/ nyin cig khang pa'i thog na bzhugs pa la yum gyis phyi rol nas rtsa dum cig khur nas nang du byon pa la dgyes ches te rgyugs
pas khang pa'i rgya mthongs sum brtsegs la sbab tu lhung ba yum gyis bar snang nas bzung bas ci yang ma nyes/ spyir ma 'di drin che/ khyad par nga'i mas nged rnams bskyangs/
de res kyang bar snang nas ma zin na 'chi bar 'dug drin che zhes yang dang yang du gsung bar mdzad/ sku lus ngan zhing gcong che ba zhig yod pas sku nye rnams 'dis
'jig rten ni mi pher bar 'dug pas btsun pa 'chol zer ba byung bas/ de dus gcong che ba de bsod nams rang du byung / de nas klog la thugs sbyang mdzad cing dbyar thog 'ga'i
bar du phyugs ma skyong du ri la byon pas/ nyin gcig ri khar lham ya gcig stor bas/ yul zhal tsha ba'i stobs kyis 'thab kyis dogs nas sang zhog nang du 'tshol ba skad
byas pa/ yul gyis go nas 'bar du byung gsung /4 rgyal ba rnams kyi rjes su zhugs pa yongs su rjogs pa zhes bya ba ni/dgung lo dgu bzhes pa 'brug gi lo'i 1400dpyid mkhan
chen rin po che sangs rgyas bstan pa zhes bya ba'i skyes bu chen po/ sku btsun pa'i mthar thug pa/ thugs rgyud bzang ba/ byang chub kyi thugs legs par sbyangs pa/ rgyal
sras thog med pa la sogs pa'i skyes bu dam pa mang po'i zhabs la gus par gtugs pa/ bka' gdams kyi chos lugs 'dzin pa de spyan g.yas dgon pa'i slob

dpon gyi sar bzhugs pa'i dus su mkhan po zhus shing slob dpon la sogs dge 'dun gyi dbus su rab tu byung ba dang dge tshul gyi sdom pa legs par mnos/ dgung lo bcu dgu bzhes
pa lcags pho stag gi lo spyi lo 1410la/ yar lung dpal 'bar yang rtse na sngar gyi mkhan po de nyid dang / mkhan chen rin po chergyal bzang pa/ sku che na'ang thugs shin du
mnyen zhing las chog byang bas las kyi slob dpon du gsol ba btab/ bla ma rkyang chen pa la gsang ston zhus/ de dus btsun pa'i mthar thug pa btsan thang pa tshul yos la
sogs pas las kyi kha bskang ste slob dpon bsam bzang pa dang dpon slob gnyis kyis bsnyen par rdzogs pa mdzad de/ nyan thos kyi theg pa la zhugs pa yongs su rdzogs par gyur
to/ chos rje de bzhin gshegs pa karma pa sprul sku chos dpal bzang po dang / shangs pa kun mkhyen pa dang / paN chen ba na ratna'i drung du byang chub mchog tu thugasabaskyed
cing / chos rje gung snang ba la bde mchog dril bu lus dkyil gyi dbang bskur ba nod par mdzad pa'i tshul rgyas par 'og tu bshes gnyen so so bstan pa'i skabs su 'byung
ba bzhin no/ /phyis rje rin po che'i gsang sngags lam rim na dang por phyi dkyil du ma zhugs par lus dkyil du zhugs mi rung zhing zhugs na 'gal ba chen por gsungs 'dug
pa gzigs pas cung zad go rim nor 'dug dgongs na'ang / rje rang gis kyang dang por gsan pa'i dbang de dril bu lus dkyil du 'dug gsung / gsang sngags kyi dkyil 'khor du zhugs
pa'i thog ma ni de'o/ de ltar sdom pa gsum yongs su rdzogs par thugs rgyud la mnga' zhing nyes ltung phra mo dag kyang mod la sbyong bar mdzad de mdor na kha na ma tho
ba'i skyon gyis ma gos par bzhugs so/ /5 sngon gyi dge ba'i bag chags bzang pos rigs sad pa'i skyes bu chen po zhes bya ba ni/spyir theg pa chen po'i rigs sad/ khyad par
sangs rgyas kyi zhing phyi rol yangs pa mngon par rtogs pa 'gyur ba'i rigs sad pas nges don gyi chos skad thams cad kyi klong rdol/ mdo sde zab mo rnams kyi drang ba dang
nges pa'i don rnam par 'byed pa la thogs pa med par gyur pa yin mod kyi/ 'dir dngos su brjod par bya ba ni 'phral gyi mdzad pa thams cad stabs yags kyi dbang gis byung
ba ma yin gyi

chos kyi rjes su 'brang ba'i rigs sad de mdzad pa thams cad la thugs kyis nges par brtags shing dpyad pa sngon du 'gro ba yin te/ de yang dang po rtse thang du gra skor mdzad
pa'i rjes de la da de mdun ma ji 'dra zhig mdzad pa legs dgongs nas thugs kyi dpyod pa hur thon pa 'khrungs te/ kha cig slob gnyer byed par 'dug kha cig nor sgrub par
'dug kha cig dpon la rten nas mi tshugs sgrub par 'dug ste/ da ngas nor yang mi sogs/ lus la shed mong med pas dpon cig la rten pa'i mi g.yog kyang mi pher bas/ dpe cha shog
gu kha yar re lta ba 'di 'ong yang 'ong / legs kyang legs par 'dug pas thag rbad de bcad pa yin dus phyis kyi yon tan thams cad kyang sems kyi thag chod de kho na las
byung ba yin/ de nas res brtson 'grus chen po ma brtsams par sos dal du lus/ res dum re lta rtog byas te sems de gcig pu'i drin gyis yon tan thams cad byung ba yin pas khyed
rang rnams kyang ci 'ong legs par sems dgos pa yinazhes gsung ngo /6 mkhas shing grub pa'i skyes bu drug bcu rtsa drug la brten nas thos bsam phyogs med du mdzad pa
ni/rab tu byung nas lo gsum gyi bar du dbyar yum gyi las grogs re tsam mdzad pa ma gtogs spyan g.yas su khu bo slob dpon sang grags pa'i sar bzhugs te/ byang chub sems dpa'i
spyod pa la 'jug pa la thugs legs par sbyangs/ slob dpon shes rab dar ba zhes bya ba'i skyes bu dam khro rnal 'byor yan lag drug pa/ sku nyams su bzhes pa de la'ang spyod
'jug gsan/ de dus dbang grags pa rgyal mtshan bsnyel ba'i sku rim la spyan g.yas pa rnams kyi phogs blangs nas sman bla mang du gtong dgos byung bas dang por tshar kha
yar cig dpe thog nas btang pas thugs la zin nas slob dpon sang grags pa'i dbon po 'di shes rab can zhig 'dug ces grags/ ston pa dbang 'od na re drung pa 'di dang po nas
thugs rab che ba rang cig yod pa yin/ nged btsun chung tshes gyi dro skyo bsangs byas nagla khyams su phyin pas khyams kyi rtsig ngos la shes rab snying po bris yod pa
de bklags pas drung pa 'di na re/ ha ha ngas blo la

zin byung gsung / mi bden byas pas 'o na khyed rang tsho nga'i mig la lag pa khob la ltos shig gsung nas bton pas tshang mar thon byung pa yin zer nas dad par byed 'dug go/
dgung lo bcu gnyis bzhes pa chu mo lug gi lo'i spyi lo1403dgun chos kyi dus su rtse thang du slob gnyer la phebs/ yum gyi nye ba'i phyogs ded nas slob dpon bsam grub bzang
po ba'i sar bzhugs/ tshad ma rnam 'grel la thugs sbyangs/ sku na gzhon pa dang gra pa gzhan su yang mi 'dug khros thugs shin tuskyo bar byung nas nga lhags ba 'ur ba cig
gis khyer nas spyan g.yas su sleb byung na dga' ba la snyam pa byung / slob dpon yang spyan rtsa dmar shig ge ba zhal ngo kyang nag pa/ non shin du che bar 'dug pas 'dis
cig brdung du 'ong dgongs pa byung / de nas shing pho spre'u'i dpyid kyi dus/ mdo lung pa'i phu'i chos sdings dgon par chos bar la phebs de dus slob gnyer ba zla bo cig
byung / bgro gleng brtsis pas dpyid thog de la bgro gleng chags pa ma gtogs phyis gzhan du slob ma dgos/ dbyar de gra pa dpung che bar 'dus/ bya lo la gra phyi tshong 'dus
su gra tshang thams cad kyis chos bar la byon/ slob dpon ston shAka pa la phar phyin gsan/ phag lo'i bar du tshad ma'i gzhung dang nor bzang TI ka la thugs legs par sbyangs
pas rnam 'grel legs par thugs su chud/ de'i bar la slob dpon pa'i phyag 'jug kyang mang du khur/ lan cig sa rub gdong cig tu phyag bcug pas bros thar te/ chos sdings
kyi ri'i mthur la bros pas ma zin par rjes na mar rbab mdzad byung bas thugs rab tu skrag nas bros pas gad g.yang chen po dpangs shin du mtho ba cig la bang thal yang
/ zhing kha cig tu babs pa la sogs pa grangs kyis mu chod pa'i sbyongs spyod byung ste/ nga rang gi don la phyag bcug pa yin dgongs pa ma gtogs dad pa log pa cig kyang ma
skyes/ de'i stobs kyis sgrib pa dag nas phyis kyi yon tan thams cad des byung ba yin par 'dug gsung / khyi lo'i dgun rtse thang du gzhung skyur dang bshad ston mdzad/

dgung lo bcu drug bzhes pa phag gi lo spyi lo 1407la 'on gyi rgyal bzangs su gra tshang thams cad kyis chos bar la byon/ de'i sos de skyid shod phyogs su gra skor la phebs
par dgongs pa la/ rgyal bzangs su dpyid de rims kyi bsnyel gzhis btab pa dang / sku lus thams cad shu bar song ba cig byung pas sman bcos la bskyed ci yang ma byung bas/
long ba mig mthong yod pa cig 'dug pa la dris pas/ kho na re btsun chung 'di'i grong de lung pa mda' byang du bstan pa'i mda'i grog kha cig na 'dug 'di gnyid la song nas

de slob dpon bsam bzang pas

bka' bkyon mang du byon nas spyan g.yas su phebs pas slob dpon pa na re byon pa de legs/ 'bod mi cig gtong bsam pa yod pa yin gsung / yum gyi gson chos 'don gyi 'dug pa'i grogs
mdzad/ de nas thugs cung zad skyo nas yod pas stagalo'i dpyid de 'phral gyi cha rkyen dum cig khur nas rtse thang du phebs kyang lam nas thugs 'gyur te yar klungs dgon

la mi dbang ba'i skye bo tha mal pa'i tshogs pa zad nas blta ba rnams kyang dad pa rang dbang med pa skyebar 'dug gsang ba'i bdag pos las kyi rdo rje la gsungs pa na/

de tsam gyi rtsis med/ rje rin po che de gdul bya phyogs gcig pa tsho cig 'dul du byon par 'dug pas/ grub pa'i mtha' rnams kyang gdul bya'i bsam pa'i dbang gis 'byung ba
yin te/ dper na/ gnas der

drang nges rnam 'byed gsung ba'i skabs su/ 'dir bshad pa dang 'gal ba min pa'i drang nges kyi 'byed lugs shig theg pa chen po rgyud bla ma nas bshad 'dug ces tshogs su gsung
na'ang / gdul bya rnams la de'i snod med pas phrin las de 'dra la gsung de byung ba'i dus su maNDal phul nas gsol ba 'debs mi gcig kyang ma byung / nged rang gi kha mkhos
la dpes pa'i blo bskyed shin tu che bar byung / thos pa tsam la mi 'jog par rang gi shes rab kyis gsung rab la legs par dpyod pa dang / 'phral gyi mdzad pa'i tshul rnams
rje kho na la thugs dad pa yin no/ lug gi dgun de dus 'khor la thugs sbyong bar bzhed nas bla ma rkyang chen pa'i drung du gsol ba btab pas/ de la sbyor drug gi khrid
thob dgos gsung / bsam gtan gling lta bur bzhugs nas khrid gnang bar zhus pas nga khrid byed kyi med gsung / 'o na su la zhu zhus pas 'ju lha khang stengs su du zhus gsung
/ 'di la khrid gnang ba zhu gsung ba'i zhu yig gcig gnang na yong ngam zhus pas los yong nga'i bla ma yin gsung nas zhu yig mdzad pa bsnams nas lha khang stengs su gsol
ba 'debs su phebs pas chas kha khyer la byon cig gsungs/ de nas chas kha bsnams nas phebs te dus kyi 'khor lo'i mchog dbang / sbyor drug gi sor bsam yan nyams khrid du gnang
/ ngo sprod gsang don rab gsal gyi lung / bla ma gsang 'dus dang thod phreng rtsal gyi dbang rnams gsan grub pa'i 'phral du/ bla ma rkyang chen pa shAkya shrI chu mig

'dug zhag nyi shu rtsa brgyad la bshad pa rdzogs pas/ lung lta bur song na'ang byin brlabs kyis thugs bskyed che bar byung gsung / sngar chos rje rgyal

tshab rin po ches gsang sngags bla med kyi bde chen gyi ngos 'dzin gyi brtsom pa gzigs pas/ de la thugs 'gro ba byung nas/ skabs shig tu/ de legs par 'dug ste der bde chen
de bde ba gzhan 'di yang min 'di yang min zhes mtha' bcad nas/ rang lugs zhu ba de la nges bzung 'dug tshul zhus pas/ des mi 'ong chags pa dkar po'i phyogs kyang ma yin/
chags bral nag po'i phyogs kyang ma yin pa'i bcu drug pa zer ba cig yod pa yin gsung ba de la thugs ches lhag par 'khrungs nas/ de gcig pus chog par yod/ de res zhabs tog
che bar ma grub/ chos rje de thugs spros pa chung bas/ bla ma chos rdzong pas mi kha yar cig la dkyil 'khor gyi thig bslab cing 'dug pas rkyang chen pa'i drung du nga la
dus 'khor gyi thig cig slob par zhu zhus pas ngas mi shes gsung nas ma gnang gsung / de'i dbyar rkyang chen pa dang dpon slob gnyis kyis lha khang stengs su phebs nas/ dpal
dus kyi 'khor lo'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bdun/ gong ma chen po/ rdo rje slob dpon bdag po'i dbang yongs su rdzogs pa dang / rkyang chen pas gsan pa'i zhar
la/ jo nang kun mkhyen chen pos mdzad pa'i nges don rgya mcho'i lung yang gsan/ mdo sngags kyi sku yon rdzogs pas/ rtag tu bla ma dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnams dang / chos
kyi 'bel gtam gyis dus 'da' bar mdzad/ lo de'i ston ma dbyar gyi dus su/ mkhan chen sangs 'bum pas spyan g.yas kyi gtsug lag khang dang bcas pa la lha ris mdzad pa'i zhing
khams so so'i zhal yig phal che ba'i brtsom pa dang / gser gnyer mdzadade/ so so'i gser rnams bsdus nas legs par 'dul du bcug der rjes tshur sprad pa las mi dma' ba ri

gsung / ri mo rnams phal cher tshar nas

de'i rab gnas la mal gro nas rgyal stengs spyan snga rin chen 'phel ba spyan 'dren par phyags phyir slob dpon chos dbang dang nye gnas gzhan cig dang gsum gyis phebs/ 'on gyi

lnga drug cig 'dug pa rnams na re/ gar 'byon ci byed zer/ nged rgyal stengs su 'gro gsungs pas 'o na pha jo pha gi'i zla la byon/ khong rgyal stengs pa'i sku nye yin zer

phebs nas slob dpon nam mkhas skyal nas rgyal stengs su phebs/ spyan snga log ma'i khrod du bzhud 'dug pas der byon/ zhu ba phul bas phebs par zhal gyis bzhes nas spyan

dmigs pa skor gsum/ gnas gyur rnam pa lnga/ rten 'brel bcu gnyis/ 'khor 'das rten 'brel ma/ skar ma rab rib/ lam rim zab rgya ma/ dgongs ldem dgongs brgyad/ rnal 'byor rnam
lnga/ sgrol ma'i bstod pa rnam dag gtsug gi nor bu/ stobs bzhi'i sdig bshags kyi man ngag chos spyod bcu'i man ngag kam ka ni dang / du rga'i gzungs/ ltung bshags/ mtshan
brjod/ gtsug tor 'bar ba/ lam rim gnyen po ma/ bslab gsum ma/

to ba'i dpe chos rtsa 'grel/ lo pa'i lam rim rnams gsan/ spyan snga de gdung chos drug tsha'i 'breg par 'dug sku na gzhon pa'i dus nas gsang phu dang skyor mo lung la sogs

nas dgung lo nyer lnga pa me pho spre'u lo zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i nang du slob dpon ston shAka pa dpon slob dgu bcu rtsa gnyis rin dpungs pa dpon g.yog gis chos bar la spyan

su phebs khar slob dpon pa'i drung du/ bdag re shig yon tan gtsang cing gtsang phyogs su phyin na bsam pas/ dbon po kun rdor la ngo sbyor mdzad pa zhus nas gtsang phyogs su

kyi 'bog khres laphog kyang rma ma byung / slar brdeg par brtsams pas ral gri sa la lhung / der thugs ngar langs te/ rta rgyab tu rgyangs kyi mchongs/ gri chung yod pa

dbang / sa lugs kyi phur pa lha khra'i dbang / rig pa'i rtsal dbang bco brgyad/ phyag rgya zil gnon gyi dbang / sna bo ba'i rta mgrin bde gshegs 'dus pa'i rjes gnang / chos
rje bla ma'i dmar khrid mun khang ma/ grub chen me long pas mdzad pa'i khrid yig gi steng nas snying thig gi khrid spros bcas la sogs pa'i dbang dang bcas/ a ro snyan rgyud
kyi skor/ g.yung ston pa'i TI ka'i steng nas gsang snying gi bshad pa/ spar khab/ lam rnam bkod/ dgongs 'dus/ de'i 'grel pa mun pa'i go cha la sogs pa rnying ma'i skor
gyi po ti mi gcig pa lnga bcur nye ba cig la thugs sbyong chen po mdzad pas mkhas bar dgongs/ dang po lam rnam bkod la thugs 'gro bar byung nas legs par gzigs shing thugs
kyis dpyad kyang dka' bar byung / chos rjes gsungs dus dbu nas chos thun gsum tsam song 'tshams gzhung gi gsham rnams na mar khrol mar dgongs byung ste de byin brlabs
su 'dug dang po nged rang gis sems kyis dpyad pa rnams phyogs su song ba dka' bar byung legs ldan gyi rjes gnang cig zhu bar dgongs pa'i tshe drung chos grags pa'i zhal nas
ngas zhus pas dka' bkyon chen po cig byung nas gnang ma btub gsung bas zhu bar ma spobs/ jo bo'i chos chung brgya rtsar grags pa la chos tshan brgyad bcu rtsa bzhi yod
pa gsan/ phur pa'i dkyil chog gi thig rtsa 'di sus kyang 'bru ma non gsung bas gzigs pas yud kyi dgongs nas 'di bzhin 'debs par 'dug zhus pas shin du mnyes/ snar thang pa'i
dge bshes ye shes dpal bya bas phyags phyir 'brangs nas zhus pas dbu ma 'jug pa la sbyor TIka'i cig brtsams/ der bzhugasaring la dbang khrid lung 'bel gtam gyi dri ba'i
'phra bcad pa rnams kyi dus 'da' bar mdzad/ chos rje yang shin du thugs dgyes par byung / dgongs yul gyi gsung rab kyi go ba rnams kyang sa log gnam log tu song / spyir
bla ma rnams sku drin che/ chos rje sgrol ma ba sku drin shin du che zhes yang yang gsung / chos rje'i gsol ja pa bsod nams dpal 'byor la spyod 'jug gi bshad pa nyin gnyis
la tshar ba cig gsungs/ khong skyes bu dam pa cig yong / chos rje gshegs nas gzims khang kho nar mi tshe skyal/ mtshams khongs nas khrid re tsam ni btab 'dug gsung /

der bzhugs ring la mnal lam du jo mo nang gsal bar gzigs/ phyis phebs pas 'thun par 'dug lan cig rta nag ri khud du phebs pas de'i 'obs la ston pa bstan pa 'bum pa gnyis la
khyed gnyis hor 'dra byed pa la 'di kha tsam la mchongs dgos pas mchongs shig gsungs pas mi nus par 'dugangs phyi gos gyon nas mchongs pas mchongs thub gsung / de nas u
rgyan rdzong na chos rje rgyal sras pa'i dngos slob chos rje nam mkha' grags pa zhes bya ba'i skyes bu dam pa cig bzhugs pa mjal du phebs/ dus rtag par sku mtshams su bzhugs
nas mjal kha bug sgo la 'ong ba cig 'dug nang du gsung nas thog rgyud de nang du phebs/ chos rje rgyal sras pa'i bka' 'bum thor bu ba dpal ye'i zin bris dang bcas pa
gsan/ zhag gsum gyi bar du bzhugs/ mtshan mo 'du khang cig 'dug der bzhugs/ de na rgas po cig kyang bzhugs 'dug pas gsung glengs mang du byung ba'i mtshan mo zhig khong ngu
zhing 'dugakhyed bshum gyi yod pa min la che gsungs pas khong na re bdag la dang po a khu cig yod pa de na re ngas brgyags skyal gyi khyod rang slob gnyer gyis zer khong
gi drin 'khur babs nga rangagis brgyags btsal ba dga' bsam nas ma nyan/ nga bong rgan 'dra ba cig byung / nyid sku na gzhon pa nas 'di 'dra'i sku yon tanayong ba zer/
gar phyin du thams cad kyis yon tan yod par mthong yong ba cig byung gsung / chos rje nam grags pas khyed la 'kho ste 'ong gsung nas la stod dbang rgyal gyi rtags yig cig
gnang / de'i ston gyi bar du sgrol mar bzhugs nas de nas byang chen du phebs/ de ma thag tu jo mo nang skor du phebs/ phyir lam brag ram du bzhugs/ de nas bo dong du zhag
gsum bzhugs shing / bya rgod gshongs kyi thugs rje chen po mjal du byon pas lha sa'i bcu gcig zhal de 'dra bar mthong byung gsung / spyi bo lhas pa'i mkhan po de'i spyil
po cig 'dug pa der bzhugs/ khong la dpe cha'i sbrags chen po 'dug pas phor pa cig phul nas dpe cha cig slangs pas gcig khyer zer/

'dams chog gam gsungs pas 'o na phor pa rang khyer zer bas/ las 'brel gang yod cig shog dgongs nas po ti gcig 'then pas zhi byed skam lugs kyi skabs dang gi gdams pa cig byung
gsung / de nas snar thang du bzhud pa'i lam stag la'i rgyab na tshur phebs ba'i tshe/ chos rje rong ston smra ba'i seng ge chen po dpon slob rnams kyang la stod lho byang
nas/ phyir dbus phyogs su 'byon pa dang lhan du 'dzom byung / chos rje khong rang chibs pa cig la chibs pa'i 'phral du phebs/ gang nas yin gsung ba'i dri rtog mang du
mdzad cing 'dug pa lo rgyus mang du zhus pas zhal kyal shin du 'phel bar byung / khong rang chibs pa'i srab mda' bzung ba des kha lo mi mdzad par g.yas g.yon du kyog dgos
dus/ phyag gi khu tshur rta'i 'gram pa la brdeg rta lcags gis mi bskul bar khu tshur gyis bskul 'dug pas mdzad lugs la nyams dga' zhing mos par yang byung gsung / de nas
phag lo'i dgun du song ba'i tshe don gtan nas med par dbus su phebs snying shin tu 'dod par byung bas phyag dpe mang du yod pa rnams snar thang la sogs su bzhag ste/ chos
rje rong po'i phyags phyir byon pas khong dpon slob rnams rin dpungs pas chos bar bteg nas rong du kyog po dgon par bzhugs/ der chos rje rong po la phyag dang chos 'brel
yang mdzad/ phyags phyir bzhugs nas/ phar phyin rtsa shes dbu ma'i bsdus pa chos rje rang gis mdzad pa spyod 'jug rnams gsan/ de nas g.yung pas spyan drangs nas dben
dmar du phebs ba'i phyags phyir yang byon/ dben dmar gyi bla ma cig gshegs pa'i gdung lo dus su sbyangs pa'i tshe chos lung mkhan chen bsod rin pa spyan drangs 'dug chos
rje rong po ba dpon slob kyang spyan drangs pa'i gral du mkhan chen bsod rin pa de 'bri gung dpal 'dzin gyi grogs mched du 'dug pas/ 'phros gtam gyi zhor la/ rnying ma la
zhal mang du gtong zhing 'dug khyad par gsang snying na/ tsheg ni shes rab ming du smra/ zer ba yod/ rgya gar yi ge la tsheg mi yod/ des kyang rgya gar ma min par grub zer
bas/ gzhan sus kyang lan mi gsung pa la/ de'i

lan mdzad de/ dpung bzang nas/ bzlas brjod byed tshe mi dal mi myur zhing / gug bkyed tsheg bar glad kor nyams pa min/ zhes tsheg bar yod par yang gsungs 'dug ngo bo nyid med
pas mdzad pa'i mdo sde rgyan gyi 'grel bshad na yang / i ni dbang phyug chen po 'o zhes bya ba ni yi ge gcig ma yin te/ tsheg gis bcad par bya ba'i phyir ro/ zhes bshad
'dug pa gsungs pas khong ci yang mi gsung / yang khong na re dus yin na 'dus byas yin pas khyab pa la/ gsang snying pa rnams 'dus ma byas kyi dus khas len par 'dug zer
bas/ gsang snying na 'dus ma byas kyi dus bya ba bshad pa med/ dus gsum gyi stengs su 'byung bar ma nges pa zhes bya ba zhig dang bzhir bshad de/ de ma 'ongs pa la 'byung
nges cig dang ma nges pa cig gnyis su phye ba yin gsungs pas yang ci mi gsung par 'dug yang khong na re/ theg brgyad zil gyis gnon pa'i phyir/ phag mos shAka thub gdan du
byas/ zer ba yod zer bas/ rnam snang mngon byang gi dkyil 'khor na shAkya thub pa dkyil 'khor gyi zur du phud nas gtso bo rnam snang mi skya des byas pa yod pa gsungs pas
de la'ang ci mi gsung / chos rje blo mchog pa gral der byon yod pa na re nang nas rgyag bzang po 'dug ste/ lar gyi de 'dra'i rdzong 'dzin dka' gsung / lan phyi ma de blo
bzos lta bur btab/ khong rang ni ci yang mi gsung / tsheg rgya dpe la lar yang 'dugathams cad la yod pa'i nges pa mi 'dug ste/ de'i skyon bzung ma bzung med/ dus la'ang
'dus ma byas kyi dus yong mi yong las 'dus ma byas kyi 'khor ba yod par yang dpal phreng gi mdo las byung ste de dus de'i lan ni ma btab gsung / de res chos rje rong chen
pa'i gsung chos kyi skyar chag pa yang mdzad/ de na drung lo tsA ba phebs yod pa'i zhal nas chos rje rong po'i bshad pa'i sgros cig la bstod ra mdzad cing 'dug pas mkhyen
rabs 'di tsam la chos skad de tsam la thugs dngangs mi dgos zhus pas 'o na nyid kyis gang yin cig la da lta rang Tika brtsoms dang gsung byung bas/ dbu ma lag

tshad kyi 'grel pa brtsams/ de nas lo gsar du nye ba na zla med du yar klungs su phebs/ yum la sogs pa rnams yul don nas 'dug pas/ khong rnams kyi bya ba'i gnyer kha mdzad
dgos byung nas snar thang du yar phebs rtsis bshol te phyag dpe rnams len du btang / byi ba lo'i 1420lodpyid lha khang steng phyag 'bul la phebs/ bgres su ma songabar 'dug
pa thugs la btags zhus pas/ 'di kha las rgan du 'gro ma shes pa yin med gsung / shin du dgyes pa'i stobs kyis dpon slob 'bel gtam kho nas dus 'da' bar mdzad pas a khu dge
slong gis ja nag gi gzhur chu skol kyogs gang khyer byung nas dpon slob gnyis po la bstan nas da 'di la ci 'dug pa/ ngas kyang sun bco brgyad kyi bar du btungs/ 'dis sun
nyi shu rtsa gnyis song zer ba yang yod/ de nas slob dpon ston blo bas sbyin bdag mdzad nas nam yin du lha khang stengs su phebs pas chog pas lha khang steng pa ma gshegs
bar du lan mang du byon nas srog 'dzin gyi khrid/ ngo sprod yang dag don gsal/ tshe dpag med grub rgyal ma'i khrid/ rta mgrin lha bzhi'i dbang / phur pa man ngag drug
pa'i dbang / rta mgrin yang gsang khros pa'i dbang dang / de'i gter chos po ti/ zhi byed brgyud pa phyi ma'i blo sbyongagi dbang / zhang blon gyi rjes gnang dang gdams skor
po ti gcig mdo ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyal po/ phyag rdor bka' 'bum la sogs pa mang du gsan/ lung la sogs pa mdzad pa'i skabs su dor ma hrul po rgyus kyis gon zer ba der
'dug gsung nas spyan gyis cher mi gzigs bzhin du chos rnams gsungs/ slob dpon ston blo ba thugs 'jog pa'i stobs kyis khong gshegs rjes su bya ba rnams gnang bar zhus pas
bya ba thams cad mdzad pas nye gnas shig yong pa sems 'khangs pa'ang byung / phyis lan cig khos bzod par gsol nas/ ja zhus 'bul ba byas pa bzhes pas chos rje lha khang stengs
pa'i gsung nas khyed kyis kho'i ja bzhes sam gsung / btungs lags zhus pas de legs/ yun ring khro ba dpal ldan bla ma min/ zer ba yin gsung / gdan sa ba sangs rgyas
rgyal mtshan pas chos kyi dri ba mang du zhu ba rnams kyi lan legs par btab pas/ khong yang dgyes te phyi rol gyi grog kha 'dra ba rer bzhugs

nas chos gtam mang du mdzad/ lan cig lha khang stengs pa'i gsung nas gdan sa ba la khyed kyis gar phyin gsung / ngas drung pa dang 'bel gtam byas pa lags zhus pas/ khong gi
dus 'khor chos rje phyogs pa dang mthun par 'dug gam gsung / mi mthun par 'dug lags zhus pas de ci yin nam mthun pa cig 'ong thang ba la/ khong skye ba snga ma dus 'khor
mkhyen pa cig yin par 'dug gsung skad/ de thugs bden par 'dug dus 'khor slob pa la tshegs ma byung / de dang 'dra bar gsang 'dus 'di yang skye ba snga ma slob myong 'dug
de'i don gyis slob pa la tshegs ma byung gsung gdan sa bas lha khang steng pa'i drung du nga phar phyin cig khong la zhu ba yin zhus pas dus 'khor rang la nan chags mdzod/
da ltar gyi phar tshad pa 'di rnams la chos kyi mgo rtsa mi 'ong bar 'dug da lta'i phar tshad pas dus 'khor gyi mdor bsdus dang po yang dga' gsung 'dug chos rje lha khang
stengs pa rang shin du thugs rjes 'dzin pa'i stobs kyis/ mched zla dbon po gra pa thams cad thugs dgyes par byung ba yin/ spyir bla ma thams cad sku drin che/ khyad par
chos rje 'di shin du sku drin che ba yin/ da ltar tshe ring po yong ba 'di yang khong gi tshe sgrub cig gnang ba de'i yon tan yin pa 'dra/ lar gyi bdag gi bla ma de yab
mes rim pa thams cad kyang thugs dam dang sku yon tan che/ khyad par chos rje rin po che rang sku na gzhon nu la rab tu byung nas tshul khrims phun sum tshogs pa dang ldan/
dang por phar tshad kyi yon tan thams cad legs par bcad/ rnying ma'i bka' gter gnyis ka'i mkhyen pa rgya che gsar ma'i dus 'khor la sogs pa'i rgyud dang sgrub thabs
la sogs pa du ma mkhyen/ kun mkhyen chen po jo mo nang pa dang / chos rje bla ma dam pa dang / lo chen byang rtse dang / chos rje phyogs pa la sogs pa'i skyes bu dam pa mang
du bsten/ dus 'khor gsung bas sku 'khor na dus 'khor 'chad mkhan yang gsum bzhi tsam yod/ khrid rgyun du gnang bas khang pa rnams na mun khang med pa cher mod/ gra ba
thams cad la nyams bzang po skyong rgyu'angayod/ bla ma la gus pa yang zhe thag pa nas byed/ chos rje rin po che sku skye snga ma dga' ldan nas 'phos par byed

pas thugs ngang rgyud bzang / sku drung na yun du bsdad pa dag gis kyang thugs khros pa mthong ma myong ba yin/ mi shi nas med na ma gtogs da ltar ba'i mi'i skyon brjod gtan
nas mi mdzad gsung nas gus pa chen po mdzad pa yin no/ dgung lo nyi shu rtsa dgu bzhes pa byi ba lo'i 1420lodpyid/ rtses thang nas slob dpon bsam bzang pa dpon slob gnyal
du khra pa mkhan pos chos bar la spyan drangs pa'i phyag phyir phebs nas slob dpon pas tshad ma rnam 'grel gsungs pa rdzogs par gsan/ lte'u ra pa chos rje ye shes dpal
bzang pa la gsang 'dus chag lugs gsan par bzhed nas phebs pas khong gi mjal kha ma byung / kha cig na re/ khong la jo mo cig yod pas des thugs zhum pa yin zer/ nga la jo
mo yod med la khyad med pa yin te gsung / de dus gdan sa na drung bsam pa bzhugs 'dug pas/ grub chen pa nas brgyud pa'i dug sngags shig gsan/ gser phye kha'i mchodarten
mjal du bzhud nas zhag gsum tsam skor ba mdzad/ de res mched grogs thams cad dngos po sgrub cing 'dug ngas ni dpe cha kho na sgrub pas bong rgyab cig byung ba spyan drangs
yongs/ khong tsho dang zhe 'dod so sor song bas lan pa yin gsung / 'jam dbyangs kyi bstod pa gang blo'i 'grel ba zhig kyang brtsams/ de'i dbyar spyan g.yas su bzhugs nas
dus 'khor gsungs/ dbyar mjug rdo rje 'dzin pa bkra shis bzang po bas rdo thog tu spyan drangs nas bla mar bzung / der khong la phur pa lha nag dang / gsang ldan gyi dbang
/ phur pa rtsa thung gi bshad 'bum rdo rje don gsal rnam dgaspar khab kyi 'grel ba dpal ldan rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa rnams gsan/ gsang snying la bod Tika mang
du 'dug na'ang 'grel bshad 'di las ma gzigs gsung / yang dag me gcig gi dbang la dbang bzhi ka tshang ma yod pa cig gnang / khong gis gnas rnying gi mkhan po rin chen
rgyal mtshan la gsan par 'dug gsung / gzhan yang khong la gu ru drag po'i dbang dang sgrub skor mang du bzhugs 'dug pa rnams kyang zhus/ de'i ston kun bzang rdzong zhes bya
ba'i ri khrod du bzhugs nas gshin rje gshed la thugs dam du mdzad pas/ thugs kyi nges shes la byin brlabs gnas de nyid du yang

byung / de nas phyi zhig na ni de'i byin brlabs chen po byung bar go gsung / der thugs dwangs nas rgyal bzang rin rgyal grongs pa zings ba'i mnal lam byung / de nas rtses thang
gi snang ba khra mor bzhugs nas dus 'khor le'u dang po'i mjug gi go sla'i Tika ngang mo rnam rtsen yang brtsams/ nam rdzong stengs pa shAkya don grub gyis zhabs tog
legs par byas nas nam rdzong stengs su'ang thogs re bzhugs dus/ phyis khong shin du dad de mi gzhan dang nged kyi chos rje gnyis mi 'dra/ lo skor bcu gnyis rang la'ang byi
ba byi bar mi gcig glang glang du mi gcig zer ba'ang yod/ dga' ldan gling gi bla ma yon tan lhun grub pa'i sar phebs nas gsung rab kyi 'bel gtam mang du mdzad/ khong na

/ spyi chos gsung ba rnams kyang gsan/ gsang 'dus rim lnga'i bshad pa cig zhus pas 'di la nged rang tshe pho tshod su tsha yin gsung nas gnang / chos rje de jo bo shin
du bzang / grub mtha'i phyogs zhen yang chung / zhal nas kyang thog ma med pa nas kyi dngos 'dzin gyi 'ching bas chog de'i stengs su grub mtha'i 'ching ba'i snon ma mi
dgos gsung / 'phral du ni chos khri khar phag phag dang zhal pho mang po mdzad cis mkhyen rab dang jo bo bzang ba sogs kyi tshab du ma

gsung ba thos so/ thang po che pa'i bla ma nyi ma ba la thub pa dgongs rgyan gyi lung cig zhus pas khong nga la lung med gsung ste gser khang pa'i phyogs mthong gis mi gnang
bar 'dug gsung / de rjes ston khar song ba dang / drung lo tsa ba'i gsung nas chos rje sgrol ma ba de yang phebs yod par 'dug gsung bas gzigs su byon pas/ rtses thang gi

yang sgyu 'phrul zhi khro/ dong sprugs/ tshe bdag la sogs pa'i dbang mang po dang / gsang snying lam rim dang bcas pa'i bshad pa dang lung mang po mdzad pa phal che ba
dang / kha cig gis gshin rje kha thun gyi skor rnams zhus pa'i zhar la/ de'i chos skor brgyad tsam gyi lung yang gsan/ 'bul ba bsnyen bkur lan gnyis tsam zhus/ lan cig rab
brtan gling na bzhugs 'dug pas phyag 'bul du phebs pas stag rtse ba dang yang yon mched kyi 'brel de nas byung ba yin/ stag gi lo 1422lola sgo mo rin po che bzang po dpal
ba sne'u gdong rtse na bzhugs pa la gzungs gra lnga'i dbang lo tsA ba rin rnam pa'i yig cha la brten pa dang / gter ma'i tshe sgrub 'di bran ka dpal yon gyis sgrubs pa'i

gzigs/ de'i don la thugs legs par zhugs nas zhag bdun bdun gyi bar du mnal med pa yang byung 'dug gsung / glang lung pa'i zhal nas slob dpon pa/ rjes thob dang rjes shes

ci yang bka' mi gnang / de nyin gsung bar mi bzhed pa dang thug pa yin/ rgyud bla'i 'grel ba na/ rgyas par bkod tshar 'dug pas med dgag la mi bzhed par 'dug gsung / de nas

par gtan la 'bebs par zhus pas/ rkyang chen pa thugs spros pa chung ba'i stobs kyis yongs su rdzogs par ni ma song / rkyang chen pa lugs bstod na bla ma dbon pa zhes bya
ba cig bzhugs pa mjal du phebs gsung bas de'i phyag phyir phebs nas dbon pa la gza'i skor rnams zhus pas/ bsgom bzlas cig gnang nas me phar phus pas sma ra tshur tshig

/ chos rje rong po la klu dbang rgyal po'i sgrub thabs klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa yang gsan/ de dus gzhis kha gong dkar na/ dbang grags pa rgyal mtshan phebs pa la/ phyag

dbang / 'chi med 'khrul 'khor gyi lung

ma gsungs/ de nas nyin cig khyed la bla ma cig dang thug cig yod pa e yin/ gsungs pas de ci lags zer/ 'di bzhin 'ong gi 'dug gsungs pas med zer/ yang yod par 'dug gsungs

/ spyan snga rin po che bsam gyis mi khyab/ phyag tsha gnang ba dang thugs dam 'khobs/ gzims chung du sku ngal gso dus mnal dum re gnang / mnal gyi ngang de kha la thugs

du

res byang rtse ba la sogs pa'i zla bo mang du yod pas thugs so ma bsod pa 'dra/ rtag tu thugs dam mdzad pas sku lus las su rung nas/ nyin rangs par gsol ja gsol yang sku
khams gsang thebs res zhag re thub/ gsol zhib kyang 'bul ba gang snga nas bzhes/ lar gyi ngo mtshar che khong phyag rgya chen po'i lta ba 'di ngas kyang blos mi gtong /
khos kyang nga blos gtong mi 'ong / dge ldan pa'i ngang tshugs 'di ngas kyang kho blos mi gtong / khos kyang nga blos gtong mi 'ong gsung nas ngang tshugs shin du dam par
mdzad gsung nas shin du gus pa gnang / spre'u lo'i dbyar kong por chos rje chos dpal ye shes pa'i drung du gsung chos mang du gsan pa'i phyir phebs par brtsams pa na/ sbyin
bdag gi gsung nas de mdzad na 'khor 'di rnams la nor nyan pa cig mi 'ong gsung nas shol bsam thon pa yin gsung / 'bru mdar gshed dmar gyi dbang yang legs par gnang /
de nas yar phebs par bzhed pa na sbyin bdag sku mched thams cad kyis gzhi phab nas bzhugs par zhus na'ang ma bzhugs/ de res dwags po phyogs su bzhugs pa'i tshe rang don

gzigs rtog dang ting nge 'dzin gyi rim pa yang shin du 'phel/ gzhan don dbang khrid bshad pa'i rim pa'ang dum re mdzad/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen che phra thams cad dang 'bel ba'i
gtam gyis dus 'das/ khyad par slob dpon bsod bkras pa de dang po mtshan nyid kyi gra sa chen po rnams su sbyangs pa chen po mdzad pas yon tan che yang grub mtha'i phyogs
zhen dang khyad par du sgom chen pa la brnyas pa chen po byed pa la legs par bshad pas dag pa'i snang ba phyogs med du bkod nas/ dgung lo zhe dgu bzhes pa spre'u lo'i
dgun yar klungs su phebs/ de nas sngar phyag mi 'tshal ba phyag 'tshal ldang ba mi byed pa rnams ldang ba byed/ 'dzum mi ston pa rnams kyang 'dzum ston gyi 'dug gsung / skabs
shig sne'u gdong rtser stag lung chos rje kun spangs byang chub rgya mtsho ba phebs pa'i tshe/ de snga mjal ni ma myong / de nyin su'i yang ngo sprod 'bul mi med par
ngo mkhyen nas bka' lung mang po gnang byung / de dus chos rje chos dpal ye shes pa rang dang 'dra bar mthong / stag lung pa mkha' spyod pa'i sku skye cig yin zer ba bden
par 'dug bsam/ de rjes khong rnam gnyis 'dra po mi 'dug dang po mthong dus stag lung rin po che'i dbu lo mthing gi kha dog tu 'dug gsung nas rgyus can rnams la yod med
dri ba yang mdzad/ bya lo'i 1441lodpyid gong ma grags pa 'byung gnas pa'i bka' lung gis gdan sa thel du dge ba'i bshes gnyen chen po du ma bsdus nas smon lam mdzad pa'i grar
phebs nas rgod phrug chos rje 'jag spyil na bzhugs pa'i drung du nyin bzhin du bzhugs/ de thon rting sna mo rdzong du bzhugs nas/ chos rje rin po che nam mkha' blo gros/
chos rje rin po che lo chen/ sde snod 'dzin pa mgon po rgyal mtshan/ chen po bsod yes pa la sogs pa mang po la phar phyin la sogs pa'i gzhung chos dang 'bel gtam gyis
chos kyi sgo mtha' dag la snang ba chen po rgyas par mdzad/ de'i dbyar 'on chos sdings su rgod phrug chos rje'i sku mdun du phebs nas/ grub chen u rgyan pa'i rdo rje gsum
gyi bsnyen

sgrub kyi nyams khrid legs par gsan pas srog 'dzin yan zla seng ba'i lugs gnang / de rjes lo rgyus rin chen phreng ba/ mkhas btsun pa/ snye mo ga pa/ zla seng ba rnams kyis
mdzad pa'i rnam thar gsum/ bsnyen sgrub kyi ngo sprod/ rnam bshad/ gegs sel snyan rgyud ma/ 'khrul 'khor bcu bdun/ rdo rje mthong rdol/ ha 'don khrid yig gi zhal shes rnams
zla seng bas sgrigs pa grags byang gi zhus lan/ rgyal sde snyan rgyud chung ba/ ltag 'then/ rgyal sde snyan rgyud che ba/ gces phrug brgyad bcu/ de'i lde mig yang de'i
lde mig bsod nams rgyal mtshan pas mdzad pa/ rnam rtog yul la mi 'jug pa'i zur bkol/ 'pho ba tshigs bcad ma/ rdo rje pha lam dbyug pa'i man ngag gegs sel thor bu ba/ rtogs
ldan bsam rin gyi zhu lan/ ston pa sangs rgyas dpal gyi zhu lan/ mkhas btsun pa'i rnam bshad chen mo/ kun mkhyen gangs pa'i khrid yig gsol 'debs/ rigs bzhi mkha' 'gro'i
zhal gdams/ tshe sgrub bka' rgya ma/ 'pho ba gser srang ma/ kun mkhyen gangs pa'i gsol 'debs/ rigs drug sa bon bsreg tshul/ thugs rdo rje'i man ngag 'chi med rtsal sbyong
bdun ma/ dngul chu'i gdams pa/ gegs sel sman dpyad ma rje rang byung pas mdzad pa/ rlung sbyor gnad kyi lde migabasnyen sgrub kyi che ba la sogs pa sher mgon pa'i zin
bris rnams gsan/ gzhan yang tshogs chos rin chen phreng ba/ rin chen sgron me/ gces phreng / dung phreng / bai Durya'i phreng ba/ rin po che'i gter chen/ man ngag gi snye
ma/ drug gsum bco brgyad ma/ shel phreng / rin chen snye ma/ me tog phreng ba/ mgur 'bum chung ba rnams kyi lung yang legs par gsan/ rgod phrug chos rjes bu slob chen po
rnams la gzhan don 'di ltar 'ong gi lung bstan mang du gnang / bdag la yang rdo rje gsum gyi bsnyen sgrub bstan na/ gzhan la phan par 'gyur zhes pa'i lung bstan gnang byung
yang / gzhan la 'chad pa ni cung ma grub gsung /

gzhan yang grub thob 'dar phyar gyi rta mgrin dang shangs pa'i rta mgrin gyi dbang / gcod yul gtor ma'i glegs bam dbang bskur zhi byed dang 'dra ba/ gcod yul gyi mkha' 'gro
sde lnga'i dbang / dam pa'i thugs kyi zhus lan/ rgod tshang pa'i zab mo mos gus kyi gsung sgros/ chos rje pa rang gis mdzad pa'i dmigs 'bum/ ston thog gcig ma/ tshogs las
dgos 'dod kun 'byung / ma gcig gi gtor dbang / rta mgrin gsang sgrub kyi las tshogs rnams/ lo ras kyi tshogs chos rin chen phreng ba/ tshogs kyi 'du ba bsgrags pa yang
dgon pas mdzad pa/ rlabs po che'i blo sbyong bzhi pa/ lam zab snying po'i blo sbyong la chos tshan brgyad/ gnas kyi lhan thabs/ zhus lan gsung gi bang mjod/ tshogs kyi khog
dbub/ rab gnas/ bdun tshigs/ spyan snga rin ldan/ zur phug pa rnams kyi rnam thar/ ngag 'don thor bu pa/ lnga ldan bdud rtsi thigs pa/ gsang 'dus rim lnga'i khrid chung
gnyis/ ri chos kyi nang gtor bdun la sogs pa'i lung gsan/ de'i ston mjug kun bzang rtse pa drung bsod nams rgyal mtshan pas sbyin bdag mdzad cing / sne'u gdong rtse'i snang
khrar bzhugs nas/ bzheng pa dang mthun pa'i dbang mang du gnang / de yan du nyid kyi gcung po/ slob dpon mgon rdor gyis zhabs tog gi nye gnas mdzad kyang / khong phyag
byad ngan pa'i stobs kyis/ gzims khang nas phyag dpe thogs shig dang / 'gro mgon rin po che'i sku 'dra/ dra ba gtor cha/ sku sbyar dang gsol lhung / ting bdun tshar tsam
ma gtogs/ nang spyad kyi dngos po sa zhing dang bcas pa khong rang la bskyur nas/ yid bzang rtse rnying par phyogs phebs cing slob dpon nam mkha' dpal 'byor bas nye gnas
kyi khur blangasate bya lo'i dgun bzhugs/ khyi lo 1442losar 'phral du rkyang chen pa'i sku mdun du phyag 'bul la phebs pas shin du dgyes pa zhig kyang byung / de ma thag
phyir phebs nas rgyal

bzang dubazhugs pa yin te/ chos kyi rgyal po grags pa 'byung gnas pa de spyir thugs dam pa'i chos kho nar gzhol/ rang gi mdzad pa thams cad kyang bstan pa'i zhabs tog tu bsdur/
bstan pa 'dzin pa'i skyes bu thams cad la thugs dag pas zhabs tog dang mthun pa'i rkyen mang po sbyor/ nyin re la ja sbyor bcu gnyis lhag pa re skol nas dge ba'i bshes
gnyen rnams chos kho na bgror 'jug chos kyi sgo mtha' dag la thugs 'jugabla mar bzang ba thams cad la bkur sti rgya chen po mdzad pa des sbyin pa'i bdag po gnang nas bka'i
lung gis rgyud 'grel sogs kyi chos 'khor rgya chen po skor/ de'i zhar la rgyud gsum gyi gsang ba rnam par phye ba'i brtsom pa 'phral dang 'phral du mdzad/ de grol nas
slar yang rgod phrug chos rje'i sku mdun du rgod tshang brag tu phebs pa na/ kha sang bar mi de tsam la rgyud mnyan po de 'dra gsung / bar chad mi 'ong ba ngo mtshar che/
chos gsung dus sngon dang da ltar gyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen su la'ang zhal mi gtong bar 'dug zer ba de thugs la btags gsung / der bzhugs nas 'brug pa'i khrid chen brgyad
kyi skor la chos tshan bzhi bcu rtsa lnga/ 'jam dbyangs mgon po'i yig cha'i steng nas ting nge 'dzin gyi dbang bskur sngon du 'gro ba'i thub pa lnga'i khrid/ ngo sprod
rnal 'byor bzhi bshad yod pa/ 'khrul 'khor gyi yig chung / bka' tshoms/ dpal phag mo grub pa'i bka' 'bum las lam 'bras dpe mdzod ma'i skor la chos kyi rnam grangs bcu bdun/
sgrol ma lha bcu bdun ma dang / bcu gsum ma gnyis chos rgyal 'phags pa'i yig cha'i steng nas dbang skur/ sgrol ma nyi shu rtsa gcig gi dbang dang / so so'i sgrub thabs
las tshogs dang bcas pa mal gyo blo gros grags kyis bsgyur ba'i steng nas lung legs par gsan/ phyag drug pa'i gtor dbang thun mong pa/ thugs rje chen po rgyal ba rgya mtsho'i
dbang /

zhi ba 'tsho'i sdom pa nyi shu pa'i 'grel pa rnams dang / ri chos kyi skor las gzhung gnyis pa'i skabs su 'phrang sgrol gyi lo rgyus tshe ring ma'i zhu lan la sogs chos tshan
bcu gcig tsam dang / gzhung gsum pa nas rdo rje lus kyi sbas bshad kyi gzhung la sogs chos tshan bdun/ khrid kyi skor nas byang chub sems kyi khrid la sogs chos tshan
bcu gsum/ gcod yul gyi ma khrid chen mo/ khu sgom gyi shog dril bzhi/ gcod rin chen ba/ gdon chen bco brgyad kyi gcod/ le'u lag brgyad ma/ rtsal sbyong bdun ma la sogs mang
po dang / zab don thugs snying gi skor las chos tshan bcu bdun tsam gsan/ chos rje rin po che de rtogs pa nam mkha' dang mnyam/ phrin las thams cad lha 'dres sgrub/ sgrub
rgyud man ngag thams cad kyi bdag por bzhugs/ lkog gyur thams cad kyang legs par dgongs/ 'phral yon bdag pho mo rnams kyis nyin re bzhin bsnyen bkur zhu mkhan grangs
med 'ong / de thams cad kyi steng nas sna tshang bar yang bzhes/ gsol ja yang gang bzang thams cad nyin rangs par bzhes thub/ bka' lung la'ang chos rje sems dpa' chen pos
gsol ja bzhes thub kyi med par 'dug bdag gi bsnyen sgrub dang spyod yul gyi drin la ja 'thung thub kyi yod ces kyang gsung / thugs kyi 'jug pa cig kyang ma 'khrul ba de
chos rje rin po che la mnga' lags sam zhu mkhan 'dug pa la/ de los yod de med na ngas 'did tsam ga na 'ju gsung gi 'dug gsung ba la sogs pa'i che brjod mang du mdzad cing
shin du gus par yang gnang / dgung lo lnga bcu rtsa gcig pa chu pho khyi'i dgun nas drug bcu rtsa gcig bzhes pa chu pho spre'u'i bar du chos ji ltar gsungs tshul rgyas par
'og tu 'chad par 'gyur ro/ dgung lo lnga bcu rtsa drug gi skabs su bal por paN chen rin po che'i zhabs drung du phebs te gdams pa rnams gsan par bzhed nas/ phebs par brtsams
pa'i tshe rkyen 'ga' zhig gis bshol dgos byung / brag dkar mo ba'i rdzong dpon pa sku mched kyi jo nang bka' bzhi ba gshegs pa'i gdan sar spyan drangs na'ang ma phebs
pa yin/ chu pho spre'u'i ston gzhan la phan pa'i sgo chen por

'gyur ba dang / paN chen rin po che'i zhabs tog tu dgongs nas dgung lo mtho por phebs kyang dpon slob bcu gcig tsam gyis zla ba brgyad pa'i nyi shu bzhi la spyan 'dren du bteg
nas mi dpon chen po rnams dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen chen po rnams kyi gnas rim gyis brgyud de phebs pas so so nas zhabs tog dang bkur sti chen po mdzad/ ngur smrig
gi jo mo'i drung du 'dod pa'i don grub cing bar chad med pa'i gsol ba btab pas byin brlabs chen po'ang byung / de'i btang rag tu phyir lam ras yug gcig phul ba yin gsung
/ zhu 'brog lha khang du bzhugs pa'i dus su gnas brtan chen po sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la bya ba rgya chen po mdzad pa dpal grags pa dang u rgyan bzang po ba dpon slob bco
lnga tsam phyag 'bul zhing chos 'brel zhur byon/ sngar las su mi rung ba dag kyang khong gi phyag phyir btud nas nyon mongs pa yid la 'gyu ma myong ba snyam byed pa'i
brtul zhugs bzung nas byung bas khong gis 'di yang 'di tsam du thul 'dug bsam nas khong la dang ba chen po skyes gsung / la stod byang nas lhor phebs pa'i lam du rje btsun
ma sgrol ma'i byin brlabs kyi mtshan ma bzang po'ang gzigs/ bar 'brog la sogs pa'i lam 'jigs pa can rnams la phebs pa'i tshe chibs drel dang / khal rnams kyang sngar bas
bzang ba dang / nyi ma'ang gzhan las ring ba dang / lam chod che zhing shin du bag phebs pa'ang byung gsung / de nas la stod sgang dkar du phebs nas zhag kha cig gi bar
du bdag po lha btsan skyabs pa yab sras dang ma mjal/ khyed rnams ci la byon pa yin/ myang stod pa dang gnyen gyi lam dgag tu byon pa yin nam zer nas rtog tu byung ba la/
bdag dge bshes rgad po cig yin/ de'i don gyis myang stod pa'i

gnyen lam dgag tu 'ong ba ngo tsha/ bdag paN chen rin po che bod du spyan 'dren du 'ongs pa yin gsungs pas/ de nas bdag po lha btsan skyab pa ba rang gis ldum ra zhig 'dug
par sbra cha ther dkar nag phub nas phebs byon par mjal/ bkur sti chen po yang mdzad/ sras po bdag po tshe dbang pa ni bags 'ong zer nas mjal phrad mdzad du ma 'dod/ bdag
po'i drung pa dang mjal ba'i tshe bkur sti zha phud tsam mdzad pas/ khong gi drung skor dang skye bo rnams ltad mo bltas nas rtse thang pa de pa zhud po gcig dang gda' ste/
bdag po'i drung du phyag mi 'tshal bde en mi mang zer/ 'dis mtshon nas khyim pa su che yang mi chos kyis thugs 'dzin la phyag gtan nas mi mdzad/ mi chen mi skya sus phyag
phul yang phyag lan lta smos kyang ci dgos te dbu thug kyang mi gnang ba ni/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'i che ba kho na la dgongs par snang ngo / der bdag po dang mjal
nas don gyi gtso bo/ grub pa'i dbang phyug paN chen rin po che bod du spyan 'dren pa'i phyir phebs pa yin/ de la rgyu rkyen ji tsam dgos sogs kyi zhu ba mdzad pas/ de rnams
kyi cha rkyen thams cad kyang bdag po lha btsan skyab pas zhal gyis bzhes nas dka' gnas thams cad grol/ yon mchod shin du 'phrod par byung nas thugs bde 'bol gyis song
gsung / de nas dgun nyi ldog gdong du sleb pa'i tshe/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen bdun pa zhig la zhu yig legs par phul nas bal por brdzangs/ chibs pa med par phebs mi thub pas
dpon slob lngas la stod lhor sgug cing bzhugs so/ de'i zhu yig ni bod skad du bsgyur ba 'di yin te/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa dmigs pa med pa'i thugs rje chen po can gyi
zhabs kyi pad mar kum ra shri gus par phyag bgyis te zhu ba/ rje nyid sku gsung thugs bde ba chen po'i rang bzhin las g.yo ba med par

bzhugs mchi/ zhu yig gsol ba'i don rje khyed kyi sku gsung thugs kyi yon tan sangs rgyas thams cad dang mnyam par bzhugs pa las de'i phyogs tsam zhig bod yul ba rnams kyis
shes/ khyad par chos kyi rgyal po grags pa 'byung gnas kyis thugs su chud nas gus pas brten pa'i gtam sku drung na yod pa rnams kyis zhus pa la brten/ chos rgyal kun dga'
legs pa yang khyed la shin du dad pas spyan 'dren pa'i pho nya ba snga phyir mang du mngags/ bdag slob 'bangs rnams kyang na ning nas phebs par re ba la/ pho nya ba phal
cher sku drung du ma sleb/ sleb pa rnams kyis kyang rkyen ci rigs la brten nas da bar ma phebs/ kha sang nas nor bus de nas kyi bka' yig la stod lho byang / rin dpungs/
sne'u gdong rnams su rim pas 'phrod/ de la chos kyi rje rin po che khyed bod kyi yul du ci nas mi phebs su mi rung / nges pa kho nar spyan 'dren pa'i don du bdag dpon slob
rnams kyi dad pas blangs/ chos rgyal kun dga' legs pas kyang bka' lung gnang nas stod lho'i bar du slebs pa lags/ bdag lus lci ba nyid kyis gzhon pa med par lam mi bgros
pas bal yul du ma slebs na'ang bdag gi slob ma nam mkha' dpal 'byor bsod nams bkra shis/ bkra shis rgyal mtshan rnams sngar nas zab chos gnang ba'i slob ma lags shing /
gu hya ar tha bha re Na zhabs drung du spyan 'dren pa la btang ba lags/ de la chos rgyal kun dga' legs pa/ rin spungs nor bu bzang po sku mched/ lho byang gi rgyal po gnyis
dang bcas pa thams cad kyis thugs rtse gcig tu zhal ta'ang gnang / khyad par shel dkar rgyal pos/ chos rje spyan 'dren pa'i don la snga phyir spyad dngos mang du btang
/ dbus nas sleb pa'i pho nya ba snga phyi mang po'i 'thun rkyen yang sbyar/ da lan kyang thugs khur shin du che bar bsnams

bla ma rdor 'dzin pa la chos rje nges par 'byon/ khyed kyis kyang spyan 'dren pa'i khas blangs phul 'dug pa bzhin da lan cis kyang spyan 'dren thub pa gyis gsung ba'i bka'
lung nan can dgos cha dang bcas pa gnang brdzangs pa lags pas thabs dang stobs dang rdzu 'phrul gyi stobs kyis ci na'ang 'byon par zhu/ khyad par kho khom rgyal po'i phyogs
la ji ltar bgyi ba yang chos rje nyid mkhyen pa lags/ gal te da lan ma phebs na dbus gtsang gi rgyal po mi che ba bdag cag slob 'bangs thams cad yi 'chad/ phyi nas spyan
'dren pa yang shin du dka' bar 'dug mdor na sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la dgongs/ yon bdag rnams kyi dad pa'i spyod lam thugs la bzhag nas zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i nang du
brin du phebs pa cig ci nas kyang byon byon/ brin du phebs dus shel dkar nas bsu ba dang zhabs tog kyang yong par yod pas dgongs par zhu/ zla ba bcu gcig pa'i nyi shu drug
la la stod sgang dkar po nas phul ba'i zhu yig bde legs su gyur cig zhes pa'o/ de nas yun ring po'i bar du skad cha ci yang ma byung pa dang nam zla'ang dros pa'i stobs
kyis spyan 'dren rnams tshad pas non dogs kyi thugs 'tshabs pa'i tshe/ paN chen bod du phebs pa'i mtshan ltas bzang po'ang gzigs/ de nas 'gor bzhi chen po cig la paN chen
'khor dang bcas pa chu bar du phebs pa la na bza'i bsu ba btang / de nas ding rir phebs pa na/ bdag po tshe dbang pas bags yong zer nas paN chen dpon g.yog ding ri'i phu
stod du bkar nas lung pa'i gzhung la'ang gshegs su ma ster/ spyan 'dren pa la phebs nas ding rir phebs gdong du phyag 'bul du phebs rgyu yin na'ang zla ba phyed kyi bar
du bkag nas phebs rgyu ma byung / bdag po lha btsan pa yang mjal du ma btang bas/ nyin cig gsung drag pos rgol du bcug nas de'i sang nyin phebs/ paN chen rin po che dpon
slob ding ri'i ding dmar na bzhugs

pa'i sku mdun du mjal/ dpon slob thams cad la sna len bzang po'ang bshams/ paN chen gyis mdzad pa'i sha ba ri'i bstod pa yang bsgyur/ de nas la stod byang du lo tsA ba manydzu
shri ma phebs kyi bar du paN chen chos gsung ba dang dbang bskur ba la sogs pa'i lo tsA yang mdzad/ la stod lhor bdag po lha btsan skyab pas skyel thung la rgyang ring
por phebs/ yon mchod 'gyes khar khong gis thugs la legs par btags pa'i stobs kyis spyan chab mang du byon/ de nas la stod byang gi ngam ring du yun ring por bzhugs/ mi'i
bdag po rnam rgyal grags pa zhes bya ba'i skyes bu chen po gsung rab thams cad la thogs pa med pa'i spyan can yab sras pas/ paN chen rin po che la thugs dad pa'i stobs
kyis zhabs tog phun sum tshogs par mdzad/ sgos kyi khong gis sku mdun du sngags mtshan nyid rtsis sgra 'jig rten snga rabs pa'i lugs gnyis kyi lo rgyus la sogs pa'i chos
sgo mtha' dag la dri ba mang du mdzad pa rnams la lan thogs med du btab pas mi'i bdag po gsung rab kyi spyan can de yang thugs rab tu dgyes/ rab 'byams pa zer ba yang mang
po yong bar 'dug ste/ rab 'byams pa rang de mkhan chen par 'dug gsung ba la sogs pa'i gsung gi bstod pa chen po'ang mdzad/ bzhugs stan la sogs pa'i bkur cha che bar mdzad/
'phral gyi longs spyod rnams kyang lhugs par btang ba yin no/ mkhan chen pa'i 'phral gyi gsung rnams yi ger btab na chos 'byung chen po cig 'ong bar 'dug gsung / yang
nyin cig gang zag de btsun chen rang lags zhus pas/ khyed gzigs rgya che yang btsun chen zer ba'i tha snyad de rang gang

na yod na gsung bas/ 'brom ston pas bod ston rnams la jo bo rje spyan drongs shig par yi ge bskur ba na/ dang po'i dge slong lugs 'byin dpon/ btsun chen ye shes blo gros dang
zer ba 'dug pa zhus pas ci zer ci zer yang de 'dras thon byung de yi ger bris gsung pa dang / khyad par khong rang dus 'khor la shin du mkhas pas spyir dus 'khor skor
dang/ khyad par rje btsun red mda' ba'i rtsod lan la dri ba mang du mdzad pas de'i lan rnams kyang lhug par gsol/ de dus lhag par dgyes pa'i stobs kyis dus phyis su yang
khong rang gi brtsams chos mang po dang / gdan dang gser la sogs rten bcas dang / dri ba mang po dang bcas pa'i bka' shog yang dang yang du phebs/ de nas paN chen seng ge
rtsar phebs pa'i tshe/ chen po ser po ba yang byon nas 'bel gtam mang du mdzad pas/ / khong gi gsung nas sgom chen pa rnams sems kha dog tu grub bam dbyibs su grub rtsad
gcod pa 'di nor ba yin zer/ 'o na rnam snang mngon byang na sems ni kha dog tu'am/ dbyibs su'am zhes brtag par gsungs 'dug pa gsungs pas/ de'i don kha dog tu ma grub zer
ba yin zer/ sgom chen pa rnams kyang sems kha dog tu grub zer ba min gsungs pas khong ci yang mi gsung par 'dug yang khong chos rje chos rgyal ba'i grub mtha' bzung nas/
stong pa nyid kyi rnal 'byor 'di rnal 'byor rnams kyi mchog tu gang nas kyang ma bshad gsung pas/ nyi khri na rnal 'byor du bya ba ji snyed yod pa rnams kyi nang nas stong
pa nyid kyi rnal 'byor 'di rab dang gtso bo dang mchog tu bshad 'dug pa gsungs pas yang ci yang mi gsung bar bzhugs song/ seng ge rtse nas phebs pa'i nyin rta pa mang
pos sa skyel thung mdzad pa'i tshe/ red phu ba dpal legs pa zhes bya bas gsol ba btab nas/ rdzogs pa'i rim pa lce rtse rkan sbyor

gyi rtsa ba/ lce rtse rkan sbyar rnal 'byor la/ rtag tu mnyam gzhag sgrub pa bas/ mkha' sogs dngos po thams cad la/ sangs rgyas nyid ni rtag tu spro/ zhes bya ba rgyas par
gsungs pa'i 'gyur yang mdzad/ de nas rim gyis ra lngar phebs nas yun ring bzhugs/ bde mchog bcu gsum ma'i mchod chog dang spyan ras gzigs kyi bstod pa tsarpa Tis mdzad pa
gnyis kyi 'gyur yang mdzad/ de'i tshe ri lung sbug gi bla ma sku na sgres pa zhig 'dug pa de la lung mang du bzhugs 'dug pas/ yo ga'i 'grel pa mang po'i lung gsan par brtsams
pa na/ paN chen dpon slob kyi sku mdun du ma bzhugs par gzhan du bzhugs pa mi rigs par dgongs nas bshol ba yin gsung nas rting du'ang thugs la bcags par mdzad/ de nas
rim gyis paN chen rin po che sne'u gdong rtser spyan drangs rjes su/ sgos kyi 'bul ba dang sna len bzang po zhus/ de nas zla ba gcig tsam song ba'i tshe gong ma chen po
thugs rang bzhin du mi gnas pa'i rnam par 'gyur ba la rten/ skyam 'chad pa stengs su dben par bzhugs/ de nas zla ba gcig tsam song ba dang / paN chen rin po che'i zhabs
drung na bzhugs na bzhed pa dang 'byor bar gsan nas sne'u gdong rtser bzhugs/ snang ba'i phreng ba'i 'grel pa'i 'gyur cig kyang gnang ste 'phror lus/ dril bu rim lnga'i
khrid bshad pas legs par brgyan pa zhig gsungs pa gsan nas zin bris su btab/ de la dus 'khor rgyud 'grel dang sbyar ba'i rnam par bshad pa rgyas pa zhig brtsams pa'i rjes
su gnang ba yang legs par thob/ de res dang sngar phebs pa'i skabs thams cad du dang por de ring dri ba 'di 'dra ba zhig zhu/ 'di ma go bas 'di zhu dgongs nas spyan sngar
phebs pa'i

tshe sku mdun du ma phebs tsam la phal cher go yod par 'dug byin brlabs shin du che ba zhig yod/ chos gsung pa'i tshe zhal nas lung thams cad kyang thogs med du 'ong / bsam
gyis mi khyab gsung / kha cig la phag mo'i rdzogs rim de gsung gi 'dug pa gsan pas/ ku mA ra shri la 'di min pa zhig dgos gsung zur du gsan na bde mchog rim lnga lta bu
cig 'ong ba ma lags sam zhus pas/ de'i tshod du 'dug ste de res bud med dang sna tshogs yod ba cig la zhus/ de rjes zur du ni zhu ma grub gsung / paN chen ni thang po cher
phebs nas tshogs chos gsungs pa'i tshe rin po che bsod rin pa'i gsung gis de ring gi tshogs chos de'i lo tsA mdzad pa zhu gsung yang / de byas na lo tsA ba manydza shri
pa thugs ldog zhus nas ma bgyis pa yin gsung / de nas paN chen rin po che khyi lo 1442lobod nas bal por phebs khar sne'u gdong nas zhu ngo zhus te paN chen rin po che'i
gsung gis sne'u gdong pa la dus 'khor shod gsung pas/ bka' lung sgrub kyang don dang mi ldan/ phebs kha'i zhal tar song bas bzlog par ma phod de/ thugs mi bde bar gyur na'ang
/ skyel thung la ngam shod gling chen kha bar du byon pa'i tshe/ zhabs la phyag phul nas phyir phebs khar bka' lung de rigs nas sgrub pa zhu/ mi rigs na mi sgrub pa
zhu zhus pas de bzhin gyis gsung ba byung kyang dus 'khor gnang dgos pa yin gsung nas yang dang yang du gtses pa'i 'o rgyal bar yong pa la/ bal bod kyi mtshams su paN chen
rin po ches lo tsA ba la bka' bkyon pa'i tshe/ khyod rang sdug po byed kumA ra shri kho rang a dhi pa ti'i bla ma gyis byas kyang mi byed/ kho rang skyid po byed gsung
zer ba dang sor gud kyi pang khebs shig gi gnang byin byung bas thugs lhag par bde bas sne'u gdong nas ji tsam bka' lung gnang yang dus 'khor sogs ma phul lo/ dgung lo drug
bcu rtsa lnga bzhes pa me pho byi ba'i 1456lodgun stod gra'i sman gcig tu phebs nas chos rje sman gcog pa shes rab bzang po'i drung du zhi byed brgyud pa phyi ma'i lam
lnga'i dbang dang khrid rnams legs par gsan/ rten 'brel khang 'jug gi dbang

gsan nas sgrub pa'i dam bca' zla ba drug phul/ gzhan yang lam gsum gyi dbang / bde gshegs bcu gnyis kyi dbang / phyi sgrub zhal gnyis ma/ nang sgrub dmar chung ma/ gsang sub
khros ma nag mo/ bdud rtsi bum chu'i dbang rnams dang / mgon po a gho ra'i phyi sgrub/ nang sgrub/ gsang sgrub/ bdud sgrub rnams dang / mgon po gi gug gi rjes gnang gsan
zhing / rgyud pa phyi ma'i nag khrid kyi lung rnams kyang shin du tshang ba zhig gsan/ nyin cig chos rje sman cig pas phyag na dpe 'khyar 'dra ba zhig bsnams nas de'i lung
yang gnang / de tshar nas rgyud pa phyi ma'i skor nged la yod pa rnams da de yi ge gcig kyang ma lus so gsung / gzhan yang rmar lugs kyi gtor dbang / lag khrid bcu drug
gi khrid dang gdams pa shin du mang ba dang / so lugs kyi gtor dbang dang dam pa skyes mchog che chung gnyis la sogs pa/ skam lugs dang rgyud pa dang po dang / lce lugs/
ljang lugs/ gra pa'i lugs la sogs pa shin du mang bar gsan/ de rjes ras chung snyan rgyud la sogs pa mang du gsan par bzhed na'ang sbyin bdag rnams thugs sun dogs dang
/ chab kyang cung ma 'phrod nas yar klungs su phebs/ de'i dbyar sku chags cung zad skyes nas na bza'i dkyil du mug pa skye ba dang / rnam spyod khang pa 'bus khyer ba yang
byung / de'i ston mjug nas sku mtshams shin du dam par bsdams te chab ma gtogs rgyu 'grul gang yang med pa gnang nas zla ba drug po'i sgrub pa'i dam bca' thugs dam la
rtse gcig tu bzhugs/ sku mtshams grol kha nas cung zad snyung / dam bca' them rjes su shin tu snyung ba yun ring bar byung / thams cad yid mi bde ba chen po skyes shing ji
ltar 'ong ngam dgongs pa'i tshe sku rim rnams kyang nar ma chad du mdzad/ sman pa'ang mkhas zer tshad bsdus kyang bcos kha rnams 'phrod par ma byung / snum bcos zhus pa
tsam gyis gser ma je mthor song / phyag shul spo ba tsam la'ang ju gal chen po yod/ khyad par sku grib chen po lan gsum du byung nas dgongs pa la'ang da ni zhag gsum las
mtho ba mi bzhugs par 'dug dgongs pa'i skabs su mtshal pa'i sman nag bzhes par dgongs nas/ cung zad cig bzhes pa/

dngas bskyed du mthong ba byung nas zho phyed bzhes pas tshegs med du dngas/ mnal lam du'ang gshin rje dong kha yin zer ba cig nas zhugs te phebs pas phyi'i rgya mtsho'i 'gram
du phebs pa cig byung bas ring por mi thogs par gshegs pa'i ltas su dgongs pa'i phyin nub mdang gi shul de kha na sko ba cig gi nang na bzhugs 'dug pa 'then mkhan med
par mdang gi lam de nyid nas tshegs med du dong khar thon pa cig rmis/ gzhan cig kyang byung stemi bshad gsung / de nas chu pho rta'i bar du zla ba gcig ma gtogs sku mtshams
la bzhugs nas dge ba'i bshes gnyen gsung gi bdud rtsi bzhes par bzhed pa rnams dang mjal ba zhig mdzad pa yin no/ dgung lo bdun bcu rtsa bzhi bzhes pa shing mo bya'i
lo 1465lola khrab la kha na rtse mo ba shAkya rgyal po zhes bya ba bzhugs pa de sngar dus 'khor gnang ba'i slob ma yin kyang khong la rdzogs chen rdo rje zam pa bzhugs pa
dang khong ma gtogs gzhan gsung mkhan kyang med pas bka' rnams chad kyi dogs pa'i dgongs pa bzang pos khong spyan drangs pas tshegs med du phebs nas ljang gi bkra shis
dgon par rdo rje zam pa'i dbang byin brlabs kyi 'jug pa can/ 'ol ba jo sras kyi khrid yig gi steng nas khrid/ gzhung bshad chen mo kun bzang gyis mdzad pa la sogs pa'i gdams
skor shin tu mang ba dang / gzhan yang sman bla'i rjes gnang / bar do gsang skor gyi khrid yig gi lung la sogs pa gsan/ 'bul ba dang zhabs tog gis mnyes par mdzad/ phyis
kyang ma gshegs bar du lo re bzhin 'bul ba ci 'byor re ma chag par 'khyol bas thugs kyang shin du dgyes par byung ba yin/ dgung lo brgyad bcu rtsa bzhi bzhes pa shing
mo lug gi lo'i 1475losos bdag mdo khams sogs bskor te/ spo bo nas kong por sleb dus/ sngon nas zhu 'phrod kyi yig 'brel yang yang yod pa la brten nas/ kong po rab 'byams
pa dbang phyug grub pa dpon slob dbus gtsang du 'gro bar snang ba la/ nged dbus phyogs su myur du ci sleb kyi 'dun pa yod pas/ mjal spro ba'i chab shog phul ba phyag tu
son ma thag slob dpon chen po gzhon nu dbang phyug pa dpon slob la/ de lta bu'i dgongs pa yod phyin/ snga sor dwags po dang ngam shAod nas rim gyis phebs pa 'thad gsung ba'i
bka'

shog rten bcas gnang ba/ nyang kha'i stag rtser yod thog phebs pa'i zhu lan/ lo sar nas bka' bkod ji ltar gnang ba bzhin sleb pa byed ces phul ba 'byor ba'i tshe/ chos kyi

/ chos kyi 'bel gtam gyis dus 'da' ba las zla ba gcig song rjes/ bdag 'ol khar sleb pa'i dus/ slob dpon nam mkha' dpal 'byor la ja 'dren gnang sbyin dang bka' yig bstod

chung / mthong rgya de 'bring yin/ nga'i slob gnyer sangs ma rgyas kyi bar du mi tshar gsung nas shog 'khyar tshun chad la yang phyag tu bsnams nas legs par gzigs par mdzad
pa/ de dag ni sa mo phag gi lo 1479lodgung lo gya bdun bzhes pa yan gyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen ji ltar bsten zhing dam pa'i chos gsan pa'i rim pa phyogs tsam brjod pa yin
no/7 rnam par dag pa'i dam tshig la nan tan du mdzad pas bla ma rnams kyis byin gyis brlabs pa zhes bya ba ni/spyir bla ma dam pa thams cad mkhyen rgya dang sku'i spyod lam

nas gzims pa
