pa dpon slob byon nas lam snying par gsum zla ba phyed la thon pa'i bshad pa zhu gsung bas zhag bcu la bshad pa rgyas pa grub/ phag lo'i dgun bsnyen par rdzogs pa mang
po'i las slob kyang mdzad/ byi ba lo'i dpyid rtses thang du dka' bcu ba nam rgyal gtso bor gyur pa la dbang mdor bstan gyi bshad pa zla ba phyed kyi bar du gsungs/ yang dgon
pa'i bar do 'phrang sgrol gyi khrid kyang gnang / de'i dbyar sos bla ma bstan pa rgyal mtshan pas spyan drangs nas smin ris su phebs nas dge bshes mang po dang khrid
thob kyi ban mo brgyaskor re la/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud 'grel gyi bshad pa dang / brtag gnyis kyi rdo rje snying 'grel gnang / tshogs chos nyin gcig gsungs/ gra pa
thams cad thugs dad cing zhabs tog kyang mang du zhus/ de'i ston skyam gyi 'chad pa stengs su bzhugs dus sman cig tu zhi byed skor rnams gsan par bzhed nas yar rgyab du
de'i bar gyi sbyin bdag zhu ba dang chos kyi snyan zhus 'bul ba la 'phags pa bsod bkras pa btang bas rten 'brel legs par 'grig sman gcig tu lam lnga'i khrid grol rting lung
la zug pa'i dus su snga dro bla ma kun dga' rdo rje ba dang / 'tsho byed chos dpal ba la sogs pa mang bo la g.yung ston pa'i Ti ka'i steng nas gsang snying gi bshad pa
dang / nyin cig chos rje'i khri la bzhugs nas tshogs chos kyang gsungs/ de rjes chos rje sman gcig pa rang gis gtso mdzad pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen mang po la sgyu 'phrul
zhi khro dang / sgrol ma lha bcu bdun ma chos rgyal 'phags pa'i yig cha'i steng nas dbang la sogs pa gnang / bla ma kun dga' rdo rje bas gsol ba nan tan du btab nas yang
dag gi dbang gnang bar brtsams pa'i nub mo/ rtsa ba dang rgyud pa'i bla ma rnams nam mkhar byon pa thams cad na bza' ngan zhing bzhugs tshul sna tshogs pa cig mnal lam
du byung nas ma mdzad/ der bzhugs pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen chen po dang sgom chen pho mo dang nya ma thams

cad byin rlabs mi thob pa tsam du zhu/ dad cing gus par byung ngo / me mo glang gi dbyar rtses thang du bzhugs/ de'i ston sne'u gdong nang so nas sbyin bdag dang do dam chen
po mdzad/ mkhan chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan pa gtso bor gyur ba'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen mang po la sa phur lha khra'i dbang drag po bsgral dbang dang bcas pa gnang / de'i
tshe dkyil 'khor gyi steng du 'bu phyin pa'i rjes thal mar yod pa byung ba sbyin bdag la lta bar 'dug gsung / dgung lo drug bcu rtsa brgyad pa sa mo yos kyi ston rdo rje
'dzin pa rdor bzang pas gsol ba btab nas yid bzang rtser sde snod 'dzin pa chen po blo gros seng ge chos 'phel bzang po/ yon tan rgya mtsho/ bsod nams dpal ldan/ gzhon nu
dbang phyug bla ma bstan pa rgyal mtshan pa la sogs pa rnams kyang sku mtshams su bcug nas/ thog mar gsang 'dus rim lnga'i bshad pa shin du rgyas pa/ de nas 'grel pa sgron
gsal gyi bshad pa zhib par gsungs/ de grol 'phral du bla ma bstan pa rgyal mtshan pas gsol ba btab nas/ sgyu 'phrul zhi khro dang dong sprugs kyi dbang gnang / chos rje
rin po che lo chen gyis mchod g.yog phal cher ba mdzad/ dbang zhu yang chos kyi rje rin po che nam pa'i zhal snga nas dang / chen po dpal 'byor rgya mtsho ba dang / bu
tshal ba'i lha btsun pa la sogs pa shin du mang bar 'dus/ 'brug gi lo la rdo rje 'dzin pa rdo rje bzang po bas gsol ba btab nas/ brtag pa gnyis pa'i spyi bshad dang gzhung
don rgya chen po gsungs/ 'jam dpal gsang ldan rngog pa'i Ti ka dang bcas pa dang / mtshan brjod 'grel pa sngags don rnam gzigs kyi steng nas bshad pa/ jo bo'i chos chung
brgya rtsa la sogs pa mang du gsungs/ ston ma dbyar gyi dus su dpal kun bzang rtse pa la sgyu 'phrul zhi khro'i dbang legs par gnang / de'i dgun 'brug pa rin po che kun
dga' dpal 'byor la paN chen rin po che'i lung bstan la dus 'khor 'dir zhus gsung ba yod pa yin zer te phebs/ bkur stis mnyes par mdzad/ khong dpon slob

mang zhing yun du bzhugs pa dka' ba dang / dus kyang dgun nyi ma shin du thung ba'i dus yin pas chos gsan mkhan thams cad sku mtshams su bcug gdan gcig tsha bzhes grol 'phral
du nyi ma ma nub kyi gong tsam du grol ba'i chos thun shin tu che bar gsungs pas yun zla ba gnyis la bshad pa rdzogs par mdzad/ skabs 'dir stag lung nas chos rje rin po
che'i bka' shog dpon gnyer chen pa dang mjal sna ba la sogs pas khyer ba la/ stag lung phebs pa zhu/ nged chos zhu ba yin/ da lan gnyer tshang pa dang lhan du phebs stabs
kyang bde gsung ba la/ dpal ldan rgyal ba'i rabs te kha na ma tho med/ mang du gsan pa'i chu bos mi ngoms rgya mtsho che/ 'gro ba'i bla na gdugs dkar bzhin du rnam mdzes
pa/ dam pa'i chos kyi las la rjer gyur zhabs drung du/ zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i zhu yig da lan chos 'phror yod pas ma sleb phyis 'byon zhes pa phul/ dus 'khor thon 'phral
du sems 'grel skor gzhan rnams dang / grub pa sde bdun dang / kye rdor sgrub thabs me tri ba dang sgra gcan gsang bas mdzad pa la sogs pa shin du mang ba dang / rnam
snang mngon byang gi rgyud kyis bshad pa bsdus don 'grel pa'i don skam bshad du gsungs/ tha na thig tshun chad legs par slob pa gnang / do ha skor gsum/ phyag rdor bka' 'bum
la sogs pa mang du gsungs/ slob dpon rgyal rin pas brtag gnyis gsung ba dang / kha cig gis rgyud bla gsung bar gsol ba btab pa dus mtshungs pas chos grwa cig tu gnyis
ka snga phyi mdzad nas nas nar ma chad du gsungs/ sbrul lo'i dgun rdo rje 'dzin pa rdo rje bzang po ba la sogs pa mang po la zhal lung / grol thig sbyor bdun rnams kyi bshad
pa legs par mdzad/ lcags pho rta'i lo la spo to ba'i dpe chos rin dpungs dang / jo bo'i lam yig sogs chos rgyun chags su gnang ba'i dbyar sos stag lung nas dpon mjal
sna ba byung ste/ nged stag lung pas snga mo nas phar phyogs su phebs pa'i zhu ba snga phyi'ang mang du byas/ da lan kyang phar phyogs su phebs pa'i bka' lung yod gsungs
bas/ ston thon pa'i dus

su phebs par zhal gyis bzhes/ de'i dbyar rin po che kun bzang rtse pa'i gsol 'debs kyi ngor/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud 'grel pa dri ma med pa'i 'od dang bcas pa'i bshad
pa shin du rgyas par gnang / zla ba brgyad pa'i gsham du song ba dang stag lung nas 'bod mi byung ba'i dpe yod gsung nas sku mtshams grol/ dge 'dun mang po dang mjal nas
sne'u gdong rtser phyag 'bul mdzad du phebs pa'i nyin spyan 'dren pa rta drel mang po dang bcas pas slebs/ sang phebs pa'i do nub mchod bshoms dang / mar me dang zhal zas
kyang 'di lta bu gyis gsungs nas/ dkon mchog la mchod pa legs par bshams tshar ba dang / phyag kha cig mdzad/ de nas tsog bur bzhugs te thugs dam rgyun ring bar gnang gi
'dug mchod me rnams kyang gsal zhing chen por 'bar/ zla ba dgu pa dkar 'phral du btegs nas 'on phu la mdzad de rim gyis phebs/ 'phan yul gyi de gong du phebs pa'i nyin
phyi dro nyi ma nub phyogs su yol du nye ba na/ de'i mdun gyi brag gi logs la nyi ma phog pa dang ma phog pa'i dbang gis byung ba snyam byed pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub
pa'i sku bzhugs pa sa gnon dang mnyam bzhag can gyi steng na lhung bzed kyang che ba bsnams pa/ sku chos ser po la sku sha'i kha dog de bas cung zad mi ser ba/ dbu'i gtsug
tor kyang shin du gsal ba zhig gzigs pa na yun ring bar gzigs nas thams cad la ston pa gnang bas stag lung pa'i nye gnas sangs rgyas dpal na re/ las sgrib che ba yin par
'dug ngas mi mthong zer/ de rten 'brel shin du bzang bar 'dug pas/ de nyin nas blo bde ba skyes shes gsung / de nas rgyal chen rtser phebs dus na len dra'i gzims khang
'og pa'i gra tshang chos bar la byon 'dug pa rnams la chos legs par gsungs/ de nyin phebs par 'dug zer nas thams cad kyis bya ra byas mi nyug brang tshad la da byon da byon
byas pas tsha ba dge bshes bsod blo na re min par 'dug min par 'dug zer nas/ ri'i mar sna de la phebs byon pa dang / de phebs byon no nor 'gro ba med lung pa thams cad
snum gtong

la song byung zer skad/ chen po dpal 'byor ba'i drung pas bsu ba mdzad/ de nas rin chen brag tu zhag gcig bzhugs te sang shin du snga bar bar bteg nas yang dgon nang sor phebs
gzims chung 'jag spyil du gnang / der chab ja grol 'phral du mchod khang steng gi ka bcu mar/ chos rje rin po che dang mjal/ bzhugs stan la sogs pa'i bkur sti chen po'ang
mdzad/ de rjes gzims spyil du gzhi phab nas/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud 'grel gyi bshad pa la zug chos gsungs tshar nas chos 'phro'i phyag dpe gser ka can rang du
bzhugs su bcug pa la/ kha cig gzigs tog mi dgos pa ya mtshan pa'i bstod pa mdzad/ de'i bshad pa zug rjes nas chos rje rin po che'i phyag phyir bla ma 'ol ba ba yod pa la
rnal 'byor yan lag drug pa'i khrid paN chen lugs gnang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen chen po shAkya rgyal mtshan pa la sogs bla ma dge ba'i bshes gnyen mang po dang/ byang phyogs
kyi rong po chen po/ du dben sha/ kong pa'i spyan snga dpal brtsegs rgyal po sku mched khu dbon/ thar dgon pa'i bla ma sku mched/ 'ba' rom pa'i bla ma rnams dang / stag
lung pa'i bla chen pa la sogs bshes gnyen mang po dang/ dpon rnam pa thams cad dang / rgyal thang pa sku mched/ bla ma rdzong 'brom pa dang/ 'phan yul grub rgyal ba nam
mkha' klu rgyal la sogs pa'i mi chen mang po dang mjal/ thams cad kyis zhabs tog kyang phun sum tshogs pa zhus shing chos 'brel dang lo rgyus kyi dri bshad mang po dang
dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnams dang 'bel gtam kho nas dus 'da' bar mdzad/ tha na 'brog pa cig byung na'ang khyod kyi ru ba ga na yod/ ming ci skad zer/ khyed tshang la dud kha
du yod / khyod kyi rus pa ci yin/ khyed tshang gi lung pa'i phu gar gtad/ chu de chu gang la 'dre/ khyed kyi yul na bla ma ji skad bya ba yod gsung nas bag phebs pa dri
bar mdzad/ bya bral gcig byung na'ang gang nas 'ongs/ da gang du 'gro/ chos ci nyan/ bla ma ji skad bya ba la bsten gsung nas che 'gying mi

mdzad par gsong por smra zhing phan thogs kyang mdzad/ sde snod 'dzin par rlom pa phyogs re thos pas nga rgyal zhing bsam byung gi shes rab dman la/ tshig skam gyis tshim pa
mang du lhags pa rnams kyi rtsod pa dang 'bel gtam sna tshogs zhu ba'i lan/ gsung rtsub mos gdong zlog mi mdzad par/ khong rang gang mos kyi bla ma gong ma rnams dang khong
rang gi yon tan sogs la bstod par mdzad/ 'bel gtam gyi skabs su 'di nas 'di bshad/ 'di nas 'di bshad gsung nas chos kyi sgo mang po phye te/ de'i brnyas pa ni bcom/
khong rang tsho zhen pa'i grub mtha'i tshig rnams la 'bru gnon du bcug ste/ de la bzlog tu med pa'i lung dang rigs pa shin du rno bas/ tshig 'ba' zhig lhur byed pa ne tsi'i
'don par song ba rnams don sems pa la rab tu sbyar/ bka' dang bstan bcos phyogs med la dpyod tu bcug nas chos thams cad gang zag gcig gi byang chub bsgrub pa'i thabs yin
par ni brda' legs par sprad/ sdig pa rnams kyi nang nas lci ba'i mthar thug pa dam pa'i chos spong ba dag la/ las de'i rnam smin bstan nas bzlog par mdzad de/ dge ba'i
bshes gnyen spo to ba'i zhal nas/ phyag rgya chen po 'di mdo ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyal po'i don yin pas gsung ba la sogs pas bsam gtan pa rnams la smod pa'i las ngan pa rnams
'chags su bcug pa la sogs pa'i sgo nas thabs kyis yang dag lam la bkod/ gzhi byes kyi dge 'dun thams cad kyang zhag res gus su song / phyir phebs pa'i tshe byin brlabs
kyang su mgyogs mdzad nas zhu/ dus 'khor rgyud 'grel grol nas dpe med mtsho'i sbyor drug nyi ma dpal ye shes kyi 'grel pa dang bcas pa dang / dbang mdor bstan nA ro 'grel
pa'i steng nas bshad pa/ sA dhu pu ta'i 'grel pa/ bde mchog stod 'grel/ rdo rje snying 'grel/ don dam bsnyen pa/ lta 'dod mdor bstan rnams kyi lung / rgyud gsum gsang
ba'i bshad pa gnang bas chos 'di la bshad pa de bas bzang ba cig zhu gsung bas skyar nas gnang / bskyed rim yan lag bzhi pa rtsa 'grel/ ngang mo rnam rtsen/ rmi lam dri
lan/

bde mchog rim lnga rnams kyi lung / gsang 'dus kyi 'grel pa sgron gsal gyi bshad pa/ rim lnga/ spyod bsdus/ zhal lung / grol thig sbyor bdun/ sbyor drug bdag sgrub/ dkyil chog
bzhi brgya lnga bcu pa/ sgrub thabs kun bzang/ dpal 'bras rdo rjes mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs/ gtor ma chen po'i cho ga tshogs kyi cho ga dzam bha la'i sgrubs thabs gsum/
'jal dpal gyi mchod phreng / 'jig rten dbang phyug gi sgrub thabs la sogs/ bshad rgyud rdo rje phreng ba la bshad pa zhu gsung bas bshad pa yam me ba cig gnang / bshad rgyud
gzhan gsum gyi lung / spyod pa la 'jug pa'i rgyas bshad lam snying spar gsum dang / rgyud bla 'grel par bcas pa dang / me tri ba'i de kho na nyid bcu pa 'grel pa dang
bcas pa'i bshad pa/ brtag gnyis sems 'grel skor dang mthun pa'i bshad pa/ nA ro 'grel pa'i lung / a ro ye shes 'byung gnas kyi theg chen rnal 'byor/ chos dbyings bstod
pa/ dbu ma 'jug pa'i bshad pa / phung po lnga'i bye brag tu bshad pa'i bshad pa/ bu ston rin po che'i dus 'khor mngon rtogs kyi steng nas mngon rtogs kyi bshad pa gnang nas
mi mthun pa rnams la 'bur dod mdzad pa/ mtshan brjod phan yon dang bcas pa'i rgya dpe las skad dod sprad pa tshar gnyis/ rnam snang mngon byang gi rgyud kyi bshad pa tshig
'grel gyi steng nas gnang / rgyud phyi ma'i lung / zhi byed rgyud phyi'i lo rgyus chen mo/ A li kA lI chu klung chen po'i brgyud lam rim rin chen phreng ba/ sangs rgyas
tshal chung / thugs kyi zhu lan/ rog gi nyams snang ma/ dar tshags brgyad/ gcod yul ston thog gcig ma dang ma khrid chen mo gnyis/ brul tsho drug pa'i gdams pa/ zhal
gdams bcu bzhi pa/ drug gsum bco brgyad pa/ sngon 'gro gsum/ nam mkha' sgo 'byed/ lam khyer gyi gnad bzhi/ gcod skye gnyis med kyi gdams pa/ nang 'don dmigs pa skor gsum/
drug tshan drug pa/ 'phrul gcod/ gong khug ma che chung / zab don spyi khrid kyi gzhung / khrid yig chen mo/ nyams khrid

zab mo/ zhal gdams sgo 'byed bcu pa/ stan thog gcig ma rnams kyang phul/ sgra'i sa ris cig zhu zhes pa'i bka' lung phebs pa la/ dang po bslabs na'ang da skyur bas brjed nas
med zhus pas/ chos rje rin po che'i bka' lung la/ mi dgongs pa ga na yin/ bshad pa khag pa thams cad du skad dod kyi 'chad par 'dug so ma gsong dgongs par 'dug gsungs/ lug
lo ra sgreng gzigs su phebs pas/ 'jam pa'i rdo rje dang mjal ba'i tshe pha zad nas dngos rang gi snang ba byung / de nas zhib tu ltas dus lha bzo 'bring tsam du 'dug gsung
/ rten byin brlabs can rnams kyi gzigs rtog dang / gling skor la sogs pa thugs shin du tshim par gnang / nags gseb mthon po na yang dgon zer ba rje rin po ches bzhugs
pa'i gzims khang dang chos gsungs pa'i chos khri rnams la cod pan yang phul te stag lung du phebs/ dang po ra sgreng de dgon pa kha byang bstan cig yod la che dgongs pa
la mtshan mo cig mnal lam du/ kha lhor bstan pa la sogs pa gzigs pas mi la dris dus kyang kha lhor bstan yin zer/ rting res phebs dus mnal lam ji lta ba bzhin du 'dug gsung
/ kong po spyan snga ba la chos rje rgyal sras pa'i bka' 'bum dang dpal ye'i zin bris chen mo la sogs pa'i chos mang du gnang / dpon rnam pa dang dge 'dun mang pos rang
rang gi 'dod chos mang du zhus pas mchod khang steng gi gsung chos grol nas/ gzims spyil du chos thun re bstar chags su gnang dgos shing / thar dgon pa'i gra pa gnyis
kyis zhus nas lam rnam bkod kyi khrid gnang / de'i dbyar glang thang rin po che kun dga' rdo rje ba phebs 'bul ba zhabs tog rgya chen po mdzad/ lam 'bras dpe mdzod ma'i skor
rnams gsung shing / gzhan yang jo bo'i lam yig jo stan byang chub bzang po'i be'u bum sngon po'i 'grel pa/ sgra mi snyan pa'i tshe sgrub la sogs pa'ang zhu ba po so so'i
blo tshim par mdzad/ stag lung rin po che'i bkas bskul nas/ 'jam rdor gyi sgrub thabs brtsams/ rdo rje phreng ba la sogs pa'i dbang

mang du gsan par bzhed na'ang ma phul/ spyan snga kun rdor ba yang nga dbang mang po cig zhu bsam pa yin te/ gcig gis lan pa yin gsung / de nas gnam mtsho la sogs pa'i byang
rnams gzigs par bzhed na'ang stabs ma bde/ chos mang du phul tshar ba dang nam zla'ang re mthor song bas yar lungs su phebs par bzhed de sngon la na len trar chos rje rong
chen pa'i sku gdung la phyag 'bul du phebs/ mkhar rtse ba khu dbon zhal ngo rnams kyis spyan drangs nas rnal 'byor yan lag drug pa gnang / na len trar mang skol dang
gdung khang la na bza' sogs phul/ de dus bdag po rgya gar ba gdan sa na bzhugs pa la mjal ba'i rten 'brel ni ma 'grig nye gnas nam mkha' dpal ldan pa dang mjal nas shin du
dgyes par mdzad/ glang thang dang lhun po rtser yang byon/ de nas spo tor phebs te 'di nga'i dbu ma skor gyi rdo rje gdan dang 'dra gsung / dge ba'i bshes gnyen chen po
gzhon nu dkon mchog pa dpon slob rnams la gsol ja zhus/ khong dpon slob gang yod kyis kyang bsub phyag gdang dang sna len mdzad/ 'bel gtam mang du byung / khong yang de
skor gyi bla gcig mar bzhugs pas thugs kyi mthong yang chen po gnang / de nas stag lung du phebs/ re zhig na 'degs par yang dgongs/ res byang phyogs rnams su gzhi phab nas
bzhugs par yang dgos pa la stag lung na lha chen bzhengs pa la sogs kyi bya ba rgya chen po zug 'dug pas dka' gnas che bar dgongs te/ zla ba dgu pa'i nang du bteg nas thang
sag gi thad na mar phebs pa'i tshe gus pa'i rnam 'gyur chen po dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen kha cig 'dug pa la dri med kyang mang du gnang / de'i sang de dang po'i thugs
zhen gyis mang skol dang / gdan sa ba la 'bul ba mdzad/ mang ja de shin du zhim pa cig byung bas de nga'i rnam par dag pa'i dam tshig gi rtags yin gsung / spyang lung
chos sdings su mjal bka' mchid mang du mdzad par bzhed na'ang / 'grul stabs ma bde nas phyis zhu yig phan tshun du bskur res kyis 'grul bar mdzad pa yin/ de rjes skyid shod
ba lam nas

bkod/ bde mchog gi dkyil chog paN chen rin po ches mdzad pa yang bsgyur/ de'i dgun dka' bcu ba nam mkha' rgyal mtshan la sogs pa la rin chen shing rta'i bshad pa dang / bdag
sgrub pa gzhung mdzad nas bshad pa shin du zhib par gsungs/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen chen po 'gro bzang pa dang bla ma bstan pa rgyal mtshan pa dang dka' bcu ba nam rgyal la
sogs pa la gsang 'dus sgron gsal gyi bshad pa legs par stsal nas/ 'bel gtam kyang 'phel bar mdzad/ khyi lo la 'khor lo gsum gyi rnam bzhag gi brtsom pa yang gnang / de'i
ston mkhan chen rin chen bzang po ba phebs dpal mkha' spyod pa'i chos drug chen mo/ lhan cig skyes sbyor/ gcod yul rnams gsungs/ gzhan yang yon sgom pa dang / sha bo ba
la sogs pa bla ma rnams dang lung nang gi mi chen rnams dang lan mang du mjal zhing so sor nas zhabs tog kyang mang du zhus/ gong nas nga la dus zings thams cad bde chen
du shar ba yin/ de la lan thob gsung ba'i chab shog byung ba la/ bdag mo ba yum sras dang ma bral nas legs po yang ste de dang 'bral bar 'dug dgongs nas de'i lan du/ dpal
padma chen po'i gzhal yas na/ zhes bya ba la sogs pa phul ba yin gsung / de'i dgun phar phyin gyi spyi don brtsams/ de'i dpyid dge ba'i bshes gnyen mang po la do ha skor
gsum/ phar phyin gyi spyi don la sogs pa mang du gsungs/ dbyar slar yang bkra shis dgon par phebs nas stag lung rin po che'i bka' lung gis dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i dka'
'grel khyad par can dang / 'khrul 'khor bcu gcig gi nang bshad/ rje btsun pa'i rtsod lan rnams brtsams/ dgun yid bzang rtser phebs gdong du chos rje rin po che nam pa'i zhal
snga nas la sogs pa'i dge 'dun mang po la dka' 'grel la sogs pa'i bka' 'bum rnams kyi lung legs par gnang / phag lo'i dgun dkyil nas sku mdun na yod pa rnams la de ring
nas khyed rnams kyi go bar bya rgyu zhig yod/ nga mtshams dam par byed pas phyi rol nas skad cha ci byung yang khyer

nas mang du gzigs/ nyin gcig de'i rab gsal du bzhugs pa'i skabs shig na/ sku lus legs par srang / zhal gyi dkyil 'khor ni mdangs phun sum tshogs par gyur/ spyan gyi gzigs stangs
kyang bstod de brag khyung 'dra ngos su hur phyung bzhin pa'i ngang nas da ni nga yang myur du sangs rgya/ da ltar gyi snang ba 'di thams cad 'od gsal gyi snang ba
yin par shin du gsal/ de go ba yin/ go ba rnam par dag pa dang rtogs pa la khyad par cher med par grub chen u rgyan pas bshad 'dug gsung / de'i dgun 'ol kha rin chen sgang
nas chos rje chos grags pa yar lungs phyogs su phebs pa'i lam zhor la thugs gcugs pa'i stobs kyis mjal du phebs/ 'bel ba'i bka' mchid mang du byung / phyir phebs pa na
ban rgan 'di sngar nas gzhan dang mi 'dra ba cig yin/ da lan mjal bas sngar dang yang gtan mi 'dra bar 'dug blos thag chen po cig bcad 'dug go sku mdun du phyin pa'i tshe
byin brlabs kyang gzhan dang mi mnyam pa cig 'dug ces yang dang yang du sgrogs par mdzad do/ de'i dus na nang so chen po rnams su mi phebs pa'i dam bca' mdzad pas/ chos
kyi rje rin po chespyan snga'i sku mdun du byon pa'i tshe yang phyag 'bul bzhes pa la phyir phebs/ de ni thugs so mi bsod ba'i zag sog 'ong ba la mtha' 'gog pa'i thabs so/
de nas lo gcig lhag tsam zhig song nas chos 'brel kyang thor re ba gsungs/ bya lo'i dpyid 'bragari pa'i bla ma pa byon pa la rnal 'byor yan lag drug pa bsdus pa zhig gnang
/ de'i dbyar dge ba'i bshes gnyen chen po 'gro bzang pa la gsang 'dus sgron gsal gyi bshad pa/ mkhan chen rin chen bzang po dpon slob bde mchog rim lnga'i lung mdzad/
bya lo'i ston mjug rin chen shing rta dang rgyan bdun gyi 'grel ba/ stag lung rin po che'i bka' lung gis spyod 'jug sher le'i 'grel ba dang / ye shes zhabs lugs kyi 'jam
rdor dkyil chog brtsams/ der dbang bzhi pa shin du gsal bar 'god pa zhu gsung bas/ dbang bzhi pa rtsal du bton nas

rgyud de 'on du phebs/ chos kyi rje spyan snga tshes gnyis rin po che'i bka' lung gis phan tshun du bde bar phebs chog pas shin du 'o mi rgyal ba byung / rtse thang du phebs
ma thag dka' bcu ba nam mkha' rgyal mtshan pas gsol ba btab nas spyod bsdus sgron ma dang / zhal lung grol thig rnams la bshad pa shin du rgyas par gnang / dka' bcu ba
grags pa mtha' yas pa la mtshams sbyor lnga pa'i sa ris dang ming le yan/ brda' bstan pa tsam gyis chog par byung bas phar phyin gyi don bdun bcu yan dang / mdo sde rgyan
gyi 'grel pa'i stod nas le'u gsum tsam gyi skad dod gnang / shing pho spre'u'i lo la dge 'dun mang po la rgyud bla dang / gsang snying spar khab dang bcas pa/ lam rnam bkod
kyi bshad pa rgyas pa/ sgyu 'phrul gyi phran mang po'i lung rnams gnang ste/ zhu ba po dge ba'i bshes gnyen so sos mdzad kyang / shin du mang bar gsung ba de gsang sngags
rnying ma pa'i bla ma'i dbon po gsum la ma chad tsam 'ong ba'i phyir gsungs pa yin no/ dgung lo bdun bcu rtsa gsum bzhes pa shing pho spre'u'i lo 1464lola dben par bzhugs
bzhed pa yang / rang gi dgung mnyam gyi mi phal cher gshegs pa dang / paN chen rin po che'i bka' lung la/ da ni dngos grub sgrub pa don du gnyer gsung ba yang dang
yang du phebs pa la sogs pa la brten nas/ de'i dbyar sos 'phyong po'i phu chos ldan lta bu gnas 'gol ba rgyang ring bar phebs bzhed pa na/ bkra shis dgon pa legs par dgongs
nas ljang gi phur bteg lo gcig gi bar du chos 'brel tshun yang mi gnang / gsol ja sbyor re las mi bzhes/ phal cher sku mtshams kho na la bzhugs/ mtshan mo gzims mal du
phebs nas skar khongs gsum tsam las mi mnal bar bzhugs stan nyin mo de'i steng du phebs nas sang nam seng gi bar du thugs dam kho na la bzhugs/ nyin rangs par gzigs rtog
gis dus 'das/ khyad par lcang gong nas mdo mangs spyan drangs

ma 'ong / phyogs gang nas phyag rtags la sogs pa mi che chung sus btang byung yang de'i lan nga la ma dri bar thob/ phran tshags kyi yo byad ster mkhan gang byung long la bed
spyod lugs ci rigs pa gyis la 'di byung nga la ma smra gsungs nas/ gzims chung tshoms su mdzad/ zhogs pa gdan thon 'phral du thog rtse mor thugs dam la bzhugs/ gsol ja
dang gung tshigs ran nas mar phebs/ de'i ring la gzigs rtog mang du gnang / yang rtse mor phebs/ phyi ja'i dus su mar phebs pa mdzad na'ang / skad cha dang zhu ba mi 'bul
ba sogs ni nyin gnyis tsam gyi bar las ma grub/ de rjes skad cha mang du zhu ba la thugs kyi dpyod pa cher mi mdzad par/ zhal rog du bzhugs par 'dug res shig slob dpon
smon lam grags pa la/ nged rang tsho tshe ji tsam thub mi shes/ 'chi khar yang 'di bgyis kyi gtam mang po mi yong / khyod rang da lta'i sdod tshugs 'di la ma mtha' byas chos
dang ci mthun du gyis 'di bas long du ma song na skyid du skyid du 'gro bar ngas khag 'khur ba yin gsungs/ byi ba lo'i ston dbu bsdus kyi rtsom pa la zug rjes dus gzings
kyi dmag 'ur langs pas sku khams myog nas brtsom 'phro la bzhag glang lo'i dpyid khar zhag res zhag re khams kyang dngas su 'gro dka' ba 'dug gsung dbu bsdus kyi 'phro
brtsams/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug nam mkha' dpal ba dpon slob mang po la bka' yig rten bcas gnang nas/ kho bo nyang kha'i gsang phu dgon du yong pa'i sar byung bas/ khong
dpon slob la chos bka' 'dod mthun bgyis te zhu lan phul nas brdzangs pa/ sku mdun du son/ de nas ba ri lo tsA ba/ chos rje sman gcig pa rnams kyi rnam thar/ ye shes
snying po'i bden gnyis 'grel pa'i 'grel pa/ gsang 'dus sgron gsal gyi yi ge bzhi bcu yan gyi 'grel pa rnams brtsams/ don gnyer mang po la/ mdo sde rgyan 'grel pa dang bcas
pa/ 'byed gnyis 'grel pa dang bcas pa rnams gnang / de nas zla ba bdun pa'i nang du gnas gzhan rang dbang can zhig tu

bzhugs par bzhed pa dang / chos kyi rje spyan snga tshes gnyis rin po che'i zhal snga nas 'di phyogs su phebs na mi dgyes pa med pa'i skabs shig na/ da ni gnas gzhan zhig btsal
ba 'thad par 'dug pa'i rgyu mtshan yang thor re ba zhig gsung / sku nyams kyang ngan zhing mdzad pa gang la'ang stabs ma bde bar byung nas/ slob dpon smon lam pa khyod
song la/ spyan snga rin po che'i drung du bdag byang phyogs su 'ong bar 'dod pa'i rgyu mtshan phul/ bzhed pa dang mi 'byor ba mi 'dug na dus tshigs thag chod la shog bdag
la 'thog ci yang med/ bya ba 'di ma grub kyi bar du gzhan su la'ang ma smra/ 'dir yang ngas smra bar med gsung bas/ chos kyi rje spyan snga tshes gnyis rin po che'i zhabs
drung du de ltar phul bas/ bzhed pa dang shin du 'byor nas de'i sang nyin chibs pa rjes bzhin du 'ong ba byas nas/ slar sku mdun du 'ongs te sang rang la dus gnang yod
zhus pas dgyes ches te/ de'i mtshan mo shin du snga bar bzhengs nas ja yang yang skol kyang nam ma langs thugs dang ma 'grigs par snga mor phebs/ nam za zi'i skabs su
mchod rten chen mo la phyag nas mdzad/ chibs thog tu 'thon te byang khar phebs/ chos rje spyan snga tshes gnyis rin po che sku 'khor mang po dang bcas pas gru khar bsu ba
legs par gnang / klu khang du zhag kha yar bzhugs/ de'i skabs su byang chub mchog tu thugs bskyed pa mngon chung gis gsan/ de rjes smon ldang mkhar du bzhugs nas sgron gsal
gyi 'grel pa le'u bcu pa yan mdzad/ de nas spyan snga tshes gnyis rin po che'i drung du gsung chos mang du 'bul dgos pa'i bka' lung nan du phebs pas/ zla ba brgyad pa'i
bsham du brag khar phebs/ nang sor mi phebs pa'i dam bca' grol brtag gnyis kyi rgyud rngog pa'i rin chen rgyan 'dra'i steng nas bshad pa legs par phul te/ 'di la bka'
rgyud gcig pa'i rten 'brel dang byin brlabs yod gsung / de nas rgyud gsum gsang ba'i bshad pa sngon du 'gro ba'i dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud 'grel gyi bshad pa

yongs su rdzogs pa/ sems 'grel skor gzhan rnams dang rnam snang mngon byang gi rgyud/ dpyid kyi thig le'i 'grel ba'i bshad pa/ dus 'khor gyi 'grel chen dpal ldan bla mas mdzad
pa'i lung / phar phyin gyi bshad pa/ gsang snying spar khab dang bcas pa dang / lam rnam bkod kyi bshad pa/ sgyu 'phrul zhi khro dang / dkyil 'khor padma brgya ldan dang
/ bla ma thod phreng rtsal dang / rta mgrin gsang sgrub kyi dbang la sogs pa gnang / de'i skabs su byams pa gling nas chos rje rin po che'i zhal ta phebs pa na/ shin
tu mjal bar rings/ sku tshe 'di la thengs cig cis kyang mjal ba zhu/ zhal rnam gnyis kyis dgung lo mthon por phebs pa yang thugs kyis dgongs par zhu gsung ba dang / chos
rje rin po che lo chen pa'i zhal snga nas kyang de mthun dang / yar rgyab nas nang so rnam pa'i zhal ta phebs pa'i tshe/ spyan snga tshes gnyis rin po che la chos mang du
phul tshar ba la brten nas phebs par zhal gyis bzhes pa'i zhu lan phul tshar ba'i rjes bzhud par nye ba'i skabs su/ da lan phyin na bar chad chen po 'ong gsung nas bshol/
'di byung ni gsal bar mi gsung ngo / de nas lho khar bzhugs ma bzhed de/ byang khar nang so nas smon ldang du mkhar las mdzad/ sa zhing mang du 'bul bas de ring rtsis bzhes
pa zhu ba'i bka' lung byung ba la'ang sa zhing gi dgos pa med pa'i rgyu mtshan sku 'khor na yod pa rnams la phyogs tsam gsung zhing bzhes pa ma gnang / yos lo la nang
cig bzhengs pa'i skabs su sku gdab la brten nas zhabs kyis phebs mi thub pa rgyun ring bar byung nas/ 'do li la spyan drangs te smon ldang du phebs/ slob dpon sang she
ba la dbu ma lag tshad gsungs/ de rjes phal cher sku mtshams kho na la bzhugs/ yos lo'i dgun snying po gsal sgron gyi brtsam pa mdzad/ dka' bcu ba grags pa mtha' yas pa la
rgyu mtshan rtsis rnams gsungs/ de'i rjes su dri med 'od kyi skar rtsis kyi mdor bsdus la bshad pa zhib par gnang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnam rgyal mchog pa bdag gi bla
ma'i

sku skye yin/ khong 'o rgyal yod/ dam pa'i chos la sbyar na legs po 'ong ba'i dpe yod gsung stag rtse nas gdan drangs thos bsam sgom gsum la sbyar/ 'brug gi dpyidachos rje
'brug pa gsang 'dus gsan par bzhed de/ dwags po sgam po nas zhu ba 'bul byung bas zhal gyis bzhes pas tshegs med du phebs/ gsang 'dus sgron gsal gyi bshadapa legs par gnang
/ de rjes rgyud bla gzhung rkyang dang / dbang mdor bstan pa'i bshad pa/ dbon sher 'byung gi bsdus pa'i dgongs gcig gi rtsa ba'i bshad pa rnams stsal/ gzhan yang dngos
su ma mjal na'ang gsung thos kyi sa nas chos 'brel mang du gnang / de'i dbyar 'khrul sel gyi rtsis 'phro tshol ba'i sa ris shin du mang bar mdzad/ de'i dgun chos rje rin
po che lo chen pa'i zhal snga nas phyag 'bul du phebs pa la shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa sgom pa'i rim pa gsungs/ chos rje spyan snga rin po che bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i
mkhan po mdzad/ chos rje rin po che nam pa'i zhal snga nas kyis gsol ba nan tan du btab pa'i ngor sha ba ra'i gzhung chung la brten nas lam yan lag drug po zung 'jug 'ba'
zhig gis bgrod pa'i khrid lugs dang / dus zhabs snyan rgyud da dang / bka' 'bum gyi lung la sogs pa mang po gnang / sbrul lo'i sos ka rgyud bla'i Ti ka chen po brtsom
par gsol ba btab pas zhal gyis bzhes te rtsom pa la zug pa'i nyin/ gzims khang nang na dpon slob gnyis las mi bzhugs pa la sa g.yo ba'i cho 'phrul chen po byung / gzhan
sus kyang ma tshor bar 'dug zla ba bzhi pa la zug nas brgyad pa'i tshes bco lnga la legs par grub/ spyan gyis nyin nub dgongs pa tsam las med kyang bshad pa dang lung 'dren
la sogs pa thams cad sngar spyan gyis gzigs pa bas tshegs chung zhing rgyas pas/ thams cad ngo mtshar du gyur pas mtshon te/ rtsom pa gang gnang na'ang / snga gzigs zhib

spod ba ma gtogs/ rtsom stan gyi

thog du bsgyur 'god snon 'brid mang po mi dgos pa la zhal nas/ ngas brtsom stan gyi snon 'brid bsam mno kho nas byed pa yin pas/ mang du bcos mi dgos pa yin zhes gsung ngo
/ rta lo'i dpyid chos rje spyan snga tshes gnyis rin po che'i drung du/ rdzogs chen rdo rje zam pa'i skor rnams dang de'i sos ka ye shes grub pa'i bshad pa/ rgyud gsum gsang
ba'i bshad pa la sogs pa/ dbyar chos rje rin po che nam pa'i zhal sngar dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i mchog dbang / chos rje rgyal sras pa'i cho ga'i steng nas dbu ma lugs

'phrang chos rdzong du phebs/ shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa'i sgom rim dang / sgyu 'phrul gyi bshad rgyud thal ba'i rgyud kyi stod nas le'u 'ga'i Ti ka mdzad/ zla ba
dgu pa'i nang du sku khams shin du snyung dus/ mtshan ma ngan pa mnal lam du bzlog tshul sngar smos so/ de rjes dge ba'i bshes gnyen kha cig la dpal brtag pa gnyis pa'i
rgyud kyi bshad pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa'i sgomarim/ rdo rje snying 'grel gyi bshad pa/ spo to ba'i dpe chos kyi lung la sogs pa gnang / lug lo'i sos rmangs do
ha'i rnam bshad/ yon tan mtha' yas par bstod pa'i bsdus don/ 'jig rten las 'das par bstod pa'i Ti ka la sogs pa mdzad/ de'i dbyar spyan snga tshes gnyis rin po che'i drung

dang mjal/ de'i ston mdo sde rgyan gyi 'grel bshad kyi dbu tshugs/ dgun lte'u ra gdan sa ba chag lo rin chen chos kyi rgyal po ba phebs nas/ rin chen shing rta'i bshad
pa/ rgyan bdun gyi bshad pa dang / sgron gsal le'u bcu pa yan gyi Ti ka'i lung ma bshad la sogs pa dang / skad dod dang

'bel gtam shin du mang bar gnang / khong gis sa ris kyi zhabs tog phul nas rtsis la 'khrul sel gyi rtsis 'phro legs par bkod/ lug lo zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i bsham du pho brang
tshong 'dus su phebs nas chos rje rin po che nam pa'i zhal snga nas dang / chos rje rin po che lo chen pa rnam gnyis la/ snyan rgyud rdo rje zam pa'i dbang yongs su rdzogs
pa/ khrid gzhung bshad la sogs pa'i chos skor thams cad gnang nas gzhan la ston par bka' gnang / de'i nyin sku khams shin du dwangs nas chos rnams kyang babs pa cig byung
bas/ de ring khams dwangs chos legs par byung / de khyed rang rnam gnyis kyi byin brlabs su 'dug gsung / bsnyen par rdzogs pa cha mang po'i mkhan por gsol ba btab pa
bzhin zhal gyis bzhes nas gnang / bdag gis mjal nas thog mar sha wa ra'i sbyor drug gi gzhung gtso bor bzung nas lam yan lag drug po mngon sum 'ba' zhig gis 'ded pa'i khrid
lugs shin du rgyas pa dang / rgyud gsum gsang ba'i bshad pa dang / bka' 'bum las chos tshan shin du mang ba'i lung / gzhan yang don gnyer rnams la chos kyi 'brel pa mang
du gnang / kun bzang rtse pa khu dbon pa'i bsnyen rdzogs kyi mkhan po mdzad/ slar chos rdzong du phebs nas sku mtshams shin du dam par bsdams/ bdag gis gsol ba btab pa'i
ngor/ sbyor drug gi khrid yig ba rtsom pa mdzad/ me pho spre'u lo'i ston/ bdag gis jo bo rin po che mjal zhing mtshur phu gnas nang 'khor te/ mngon par dga' ba'i chos
rdzong gi rgyal chen brag mgor bsdad cing / dpon slob nyung 'dus sku mtshams bsdams nas/ lo de'i hor zla dgu pa'i tshes nyer bzhi'i snga dro nas bzung ste/ bya lo zla ba
gsum pa'i bar du/ nyin re ltar snga thun phyi thun gnyis kyi ring la/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i bshad pa yongs rdzogs grub pa'i rjes su/ bu rin po che dang 'jam dbyangs chos
mgon pa'i rgyud 'grel gyi mchan/ chos rje bla ma'i dus 'khor Tika chen/ rgyud phyi ma rnams kyi lung / rdo rje snying 'grel gyi bshad pa/ lta 'dod mdor bstan don dam bsnyen
pa dang / dbang mdor bstan gyi

'grel pa sA dhu pu tras mdzad pa'i lung / dpe med 'tsho'i sbyor drug dang / nyi ma dpal ye shes kyi 'grel pa/ mtshan brjod 'grel pa nyi ma dpal ye shes kyis mdzad pa/ rin chen
sgrom lde'i bshad pa dmyal pa hrul pos mdzad pa/ dus zhabs snyan rgyud/ grub chen yu mo'i gsal sgron bzhi/ gsang 'dus 'grel pa sgron gsal gyi bshad pa/ rim lnga/ spyod
bsdus/ 'jam dpal zhal lung / grol thig sbyor bdun rnams kyi bshad pa/ dkyil chog bzhi brgya lnga bcu pa/ bdag sgrub pa/ gtor ma chen po'i cho ga tshogs 'khor gyi cho ga
sgrub thabs kun bzang la sogs pa dang / bshad rgyud rdo rje phreng ba/ dgongs pa lung ston/ ye shes rdo rje kun las btus pa/ lha mo bzhis zhus/ rgyud phyi ma/ brtag gnyis
kyi rgyud rnams kyi bshad pa/ brtag gnyis kyi nA ro 'grel pa'i lung / gsang snying spar khab dang bcas pa'i bshad pa'i sngon du sgro phug pa'i chos lnga dang / lam rnam
bkod kyi bshad pa la sogs rnying ma'i skor shin du mang ba dang / sangs rgyas ye shes kyis mdzad pa'i bsam gtan mig gi sgron ma'i lung / tshad ma rigs thigs dang / rgyud
bla ma dang / mngon rtogs rgyan seng ge bzang po'i 'grel pa dang bcas pa dang / dbu ma 'jug pa dang / spyod 'jug rnams kyi bshad pa/ rtsis kyi sa ris rgyu mtshan rtsis dang
bcas pa/ ka lA pa'i dbu nas ming le yan tsam gyi sa ris/ rta mgrin lha bzhi dang snyan rgyud rdo rje zam pa'i dbang dang khrid gzhung bshad la sogs pa shin du mang ba/
rig pa'i rtsal dbang bco brgyad/ a ro snyan rgyud kyi khrid skor/ rmangs do ha'i rnam bshad kyi steng nas bshad pa/ chos rje phyogs pa'i sbyor drug gi srog 'dzin yan gyi
khrid/ kun spangs pa'i yan lag phyi ma gnyis kyi khrid yigaphyogs pa'i ngos sprod dang bcas pa/ gsang 'dus kyi nag khrid kyi skor rnams/ a bha yA'i man ngag snye ma/ zhi

lam 'bras dpe mdzod ma'i skor tshang ma/ grub pa sde bdun/ de kho na nyid bcu pa lhan skyes rdo rje'i 'grel pa dang bcas pa'i bshad pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa/ sdom pa nyi
shu pa'i 'grel pa zhi ba 'tshos mdzad pa bslab btus/ shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa brgyad stong pa/ mdo ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyal po/ 'brug pa'i khrid chen brgyad/ 'jam

dang po/ sangs rgyas thod pa/ bde chen ral gcig sdom 'byung / rdo rje mkha' 'gro/ phag mo mngon 'byung / nges brjod bla ma/ kun spyod/ khrag 'thung mngon 'byung / phyag
chen thig le/ ye shes thig le/ de kho na nyid kyi sgron ma rdo rje snying po rgyan gyi rgyud/ rtog bdun/ rtog gsum/ gtam rgyud kyi rtog pa/ gdong drug gshed dmar kyi rgyud
rim par phye ba bcu dgu pa/ rnam snang sgyu 'phrul dra ba la sogs pa shin du mang ba bka' drin du mdzad pa'i dus su/ sku nyams kyang sngar bas bzang ba/ sku khams shin

deb ther sngon po sogs brtsams pa/sa pho khyi lo 1478lola deb ther sngon po che ba'i brtsom pa gnang zhing / dwags po rab 'byams pa la dus 'khor dbu zhabs kyi don thams

ring la dpyid kyi thig le'i 'grel pa'i bshad pa dang / mtshan brjod kyi rgya dpe'i steng nas skad dod sprod pa dang / naro dong sprugs kyi dbang la sogs pa mang du gnang /

ba'i sgron ma dag gi brtsom legs par grub/ de rjes rten 'brel sgra sgrub kyang brtsams/ mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i 'grel pa gru gzings klog pa la snyan legs par gtad de mchan
yang 'ga' re btab/ snon gyi zla ba la dge ba'i bshes gnyen kun dga' rgyal mtshan pa la/ slob dpon zla ba grags pa'i tshig gsal nag 'byam dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod
pa la 'jug pa'i shes rab le'u rnams dris lan gyis gtan la phabs nas/ bsam pa las byung chos kyi sgo mo phye te gsang sngags lam gyi gnad mang du stsal bar mdzad do/
de yan chad du kha cig rab tu byung ba'i mkhan po/ kha cig la dge tshul brlab pa sbyin pa/ kha cig bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i mkhan po/ las kyi slob dpon dang / gsang ste ston
pa dang / dge bsnyen gyi bslab pa dang / bsnyen gnas kyi sdom pa sbyin pa dang / sems bskyed mdor bsdus res byang chub tu sems bskyed bcug pa dang / gsang sngags kyi rjes
su gnang ba dang / dbang bskur zhing lha'i sgrub thabs phog pa dang / bsgom pa'i man ngag mdor bsdus gnang ba la sogs pa ni shin du mang bar yod de/ spyir gyis chos kyi
sgo mtha' dag par gsung yang / dbang bskur ba dang bslab pa skyor ba'i mkhan slob la shin du 'dzem/ khyad par bslab pa bskyar ba byung na nges par bsnyel 'ong / rdzogs
rims kyi gnad mtha' dag gsung yang khrid 'debs pa la shin du 'dzang / zab mo'i don gsung ba yang gang zag de'i dbang po brtags shing / sngags pa gtso bor gyur na bskyed pa'i
rim pa'i skor shas che ba dang / sde snod 'dzin pa mang du tshogs na grub mtha'i bshad pa shas che bar 'ong ba dang / rnal 'byor la gnas pa gtso bor gyur na/ zab gnad
gsung ba shas che'o zhes

grags so/ chos gang gsung yang snga gzigs phyi gzigs mdzad pa dang / gang zag gzhan gyi Ti ka la brten nas gsungs pa dang / gzhan 'gog pa kho na lhur len pa la sogs pa ni mi
mdzad/ sku lus bsrangs nas/ thog mar dbu zhabs kyi don thams cad hril te dril nas gsung / gzhung so so'i dka' gnad kyi skabs su/ bka' dang mkhas pa tshad ldan gyi bzhed
pa thams cad dpang por mdzad nas shes bya gzhi nas bslang ste/ chos thams cad chos gcig gi steng du phab/ chos thams cad kyis chos gcig 'chad de/ 'ben phyi rol du mi tshol
bar mde'u rtse nang bstan nas gang zag so so'i rgyud dang sbyar nas/ nyan pa po rang gis khong du chud ma chud pa la 'thad mi 'thad kyi brgal brtag zhu zhing nyan chog
pas/ yin min gyi dri ba zhus pa la mi dgyes pa med bzhin du rmed par mdzad pa la/ gdul bya'i blo gros dang brtson 'grus kyis lcogs na nyin mtshan song ba ma tshor ba gsung
/ de yang bstan bcos gsungs pa la snga ba rta nag tu spyod 'jug gsungs pa/ rnam bshad brtsams pa la snga ba sgron mar dbu ma 'jug pa'i Ti ka brtsams pa/ dbang bskur ba
la snga ba rdo rje 'dzin pa bkra shis rgya mtsho ba la sgyu 'phrul zhi ba'i dbang gnang pa/ rgyud gsungs pa la snga ba ston pa rin chen dpal bzang la dpal dus kyi 'khor
lo gsungs pa/ khrid btab pa la snga ba dmar ston chos rje la sbyor drug gnang ba'i 'og tu nam rgyal la lam rnam bkod kyi khrid btab pa deyin no/ sa mo phag gi lo'i 1479loston
rgyab/ chos rje rin po che lo chen phebs nas/ zhag nyi shu'i bar du bsnyen bkur rgya cher zhus shing / rdo rje snying 'grel gyi bshad pa/ bi ma la'i rig pa'i rtsal dbang
bco brgyad/ a ro'i snyan rgyud la sogs pa gnang / rdo rje snying 'grel ji ltar gsungs pa ltar 'phral du zin bris btab pas dgyes nas bsngags pa mdzad/ lo de'i dgun zla
'bring po la/ jo bos mdzad pa'i bden gnyis kyi Ti ka dang / cho 'phrul gyi zla ba la byang chub lam sgron dang / dbu ma'i man ngag gi bshad pa rnams brtsams/ lcags pho
byi ba lo'i 1480lodgun/

dpal sa ra ha pas mdzad pa'i do ha mdzod tshigs su bcad pa bzhi bcu pa rgyal po do ha dang / mi zad pa'i gter mdzod man ngag gi glu tshigs su bcad pa brgyad cu pa btsun mo
do ha zhes pa dang / de kho na nyid kyi man ngag tshigs su bcad pa bcu gnyis pa rnams kyi 'grel pa/ slob dpon smon lam grags pas bskul ba'i ngor rtsom pa gnang zhing / spyan
phyes pas gsal bar gyur pa'i tshe/ lcags mo glang gi lo 1481lozla ba gsum pa la/ bdag phyag 'bul dang 'dod chos 'phrod zhu bar/ yang dgon pho brang du slebs/ jo bos mdzad
pa'i lam sgron bden gnyis dbu ma'i man ngag rnams kyi gzhung gi phyag dpe bsnams nas bshad pa rgya chen po dang / mdo sde rgyan 'grel pa dang bcas pa'i bshad pa rgyas
pa sogs mang du gnang / chos kyi rje lo chen gyi zhal snga nas phebs/ zur du dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i mchog dbang dang / bde mchog stod 'grel gyi bshad pa gsan pa'i zhor
la kho bos kyang legs par zhus so/ de'i rting du/ dpon sa spyan snga tshes gnyis rin po ches gsol ba btab nas/ sa lugs kyi rdo rje phur pa'i dbang / drag po sgrol dbang
dang bcas pa gnang ba'i phyags phyir bdag gis zhus pa'i sta gon gyi dgong mo/ byin brlabs kyi mthus kho bo cag la rmi ltas bzang po'ang byung / skabs der/ nang so don yod
rdo rje rgyal pos mngon chung gis sku mdun du mjal chos kyi 'brel pa'ang bzheng pa ltar stsal/ de dang khang nyer bya pa khri dpon bkra shis dar rgyas pas mjal zhing / chos
kyi 'brel pa zhus nas/ sde dpon de dag gus pa dang ldan par gyur to/ 26 ma 'ongs pa'i dus kyang sems dpa' chen po'i rnam par thar pa rgyun mi 'chad pa zhes pa ni/sku
tshe 'di nyid kyis bstan pa la phan pa dang sems can gyi don rlabs po che yun ring du mdzad pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba mtha' dag kyang / rgya ba ma pham pa la sogs pa'i gsung
rabs yongs su 'dzin pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa phul du byung ba 'grub pa'i ched du dmigs pa yin te/ ji skad du/ rje btsun ma pham nyid kyi mthu/ kho nas bdag ni
legs drangs te/ dga' ldan gnas su theg chen gyi/

chos la yang dag spyod par shog ces bya ba la sogs pa rgyud bla'i 'grel bshad de kho na nyid rab tu gsal ba'i me long gi mjug tu dge ba bsngos pa lta bu'o/ lo de nyid kyi spyi
lo 1481zla ba bcu pa'i sgang nas gsol dang cung zad 'grib pa dang / mgur glo mang tsam ma gtogs bsnyel ba med na'ang / thugs dam gyi ltas zhing gzhan du dgongs pa gtad
pa'i mtshan ma byung tshul bka' shog chos kyi rgyal po spyan snga gong ma chen po'i drung dang / stag lung rin po che kun mkhyen ngag gi dbang po dang / chos kyi rje lo
chen gyi zhal snga nas la gnang ba dang / bdag lho rgyud du tsa ri tra'i gnas nang nas 'khor te/ chos rgyal lhun por yong dus phebs pas/ zhal slob mchog dman bar ma mtha'
dag gis so sor chos sde tha dad du sku rim rgya chen po bsgrub cing gsol ba btab kyang / mtshan ltas bzang po ma byung ba ltar/ zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes nyer brgyad la/
zhi ba chen po'i dbyings su snyoms par zhugs pa nas/ ji srid thugs dam ma grol gyi bar du nam mkha' shin du 'jam pa nyin mtshan thams cad du byung la/ slob dpon rin po
che gzhon nu dbang phyug dang / slob dpon smon lam grags pa gtso bor gyur pa'i dam tshig rnam par dag pa rnams kyis mchod cing / zla ba bcu gnyis pa la/ rtses thang gi gra
sa chen po sogs su/ spyan snga gong ma chen po dang / chos kyi rje lo chen zhabs kyis/ rje de nyid kyi dgongs rdzogs kyi 'gyed chen po dang / gdung mchod rgya cher mdzad
cing / bdag gis kyang tshes bcu'i snga dro dge 'dun lnga stong tsam la 'gyed ci 'byor pa bshams te/ phyi dro sku gdung rin po che gos dar gyi na bza' dang bcas pa zangs
gser las grub pa'i mchod rten du bzhugs su gsol nas/ sku tshad dang mnyam pa'i gzims mal du bzhugs pa'i mkhar ba las grub pa'i sku 'dra/ yang dgon gyi rgyab tu phyi rten
ye shes mchod rten tshad cheb bzhengs pa/ slob dpon smon lam grags pas do dam bgyis shing / chos kyi rgyal po spyan snga gong ma chen pos/ gtsug lag khang du nang rten
rje btsun byams pa'i sku li ma bzhengs pa rnams kyi rab tu gnas pa'ang grub bo/ de nas chu pho byi ba'i lo zla ba gsum

pa'i tshes brgyad kyi sred sku gdung rin po che ngo mtshar ba'i ltas dang bcas te mngon par sbyangs shing / gdung ring srel gyi tshogs phal cher dad pa dang ldan pa rnams kyi
mchod pa'i rten du gyur la/ gdung tsha mang po sngar mal bzhugs pa dang / khyad par du zhal ko gdan sa chen po thelagyi rten gyi khrod dang / dbu thod ril po dga' ldan
ma mo'i lha chen gyi thugs kar bzhugs so/ mtshungs pa med pa'i dpal ldan bla ma mchog gi rnam thar ni/ bdag gis bskul nas slob dpon smon lam grags pas legs sbyar ba/ de
la gzhi byas sgro bskur bral zhing gsal bar bkod pa'i dges/ skye ba kun du mgon po de yis rjes su 'dzin gyur cig bla ma rnams kyi lo rgyus ji snyed pa/ sgro 'dogs tshig rgyan
brtsom la mi dgyes shing / rang babs dngos gnas brjod la bsngags mdzad pas/ dgongs pa nyid las gzhan du ma spos so/ yon tan mang po rang gis bsgrags so zhes/ snyigs
dus log rtog can la sbed dgos pa'ang / 'di na cung zad gsal bar smos pa la/ mngon par dad rnams skal ba bzang ba yin/ dpal ldan bla ma mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa don
gyi slad du mtshan nas smos te gzhon nu dpal gyi rnam par thar pa yon tan rin po che mchog tu rgyas pa'i ljon pa zhes bya ba/ rje btsun de nyid zhi bar gshegs nas lo grangs
sum bcu so bdun la babs pa/ me mo glang gi lo 1517 lozla ba bzhi pa'i tshes bcu drug gi snga dro'i dus dge ba la/ shAkya'i dge slong chos kyi grags pas/ dpal bde chen
yangs pa can gyi gtsug lag khang du sbyar ba'i yi ge pa ni rin chen bkra shis zhes bya bas bgyis te grub pa/ phyogs dus kun tu dge legs 'phel bar gyur cig// //
